Establishment of Post-War Rehabilitation Committee in the Western Fujian Bandit Area

Zhang Yan Arrives in Fuzhou Upon Summons

Shantou: The 19th Route Army captured Longyan, and refugees are returning to their homeland. After the recapture of the bandit areas, a Post-War Rehabilitation Committee for Western Fujian will be established as the highest administrative organ to investigate and allocate households, issue good citizen certificates, inspect and arrange the people's militia, and reorganize the peasant armed forces. The plan includes: 1) Temporarily preserving the original state of land distribution by the Red bandits, uniformly collecting land tax, and extracting 30% of the original rent to provide relief to fleeing owners and to operate the people's militia; 2) After the owners return and register accurately, distributing land according to the area of land in the rural area and the population to the farmers; 3) After the land is distributed to the farmers, stipulating the proportion of land tax collection and abolishing the old system of Dingliang. This is a pilot program of "land to the tiller." (5th Dispatch)

Fuzhou: Zhang Yan came to the province from Xiamen yesterday after being summoned by Jiang Guangnai. (5th Dispatch)

Seven-Province Highway Conference

Proposed Eleven Major Trunk Lines

Further Detailed Discussion This Morning

Hankou: The Second General Meeting of the Seven-Province Highway Conference was held at 9:00 AM on the 5th in the auditorium of the Pacification Commissioner's Office. Zhu Shaoliang chaired the meeting, and Chief Secretary Luo Junqiang reported. (A) The Review Committee proposed eleven major trunk lines. (B) The trunk lines and branch lines of each province were then discussed, with Li Shucheng, Chen Ticheng, Qin Fen, Zhang Jingyu, Wang Zhaoquan, Xu Xingcheng, and Wang Lun speaking in succession. The chairman summarized everyone's opinions and put them to a vote, deciding: (A) to stipulate the principles of the trunk lines; (B) to propose, based on the above principles, eleven major trunk lines: 1. Beijing-Shanghai, 2. Beijing-Shaanxi, 3. Bian-Guangdong, 4. Beijing-Guizhou, 5. Beijing-Sichuan, 6. Luoyang-Shaoguan, 7. Zhuzhou-Qiyang, 8. Beijing-Shandong, 9. Beijing-Fujian, 10. Hai-Zheng, 11. Shanghai-Guangxi. The names of each line are temporarily assumed and will be submitted to Chairman Chiang for decision; (C) Representatives from each province will prepare detailed tables of the trunk and branch lines within their respective provinces based on the forms proposed by the Secretariat, and send them to the Secretariat for compilation and printing for discussion at the Second Meeting. The meeting adjourned at 1:00 PM and is scheduled to continue with the Third Meeting on the morning of the 6th. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Foreign Important Telegrams

House of Anti-Reactionary Leader Toyama Mitsuru Raided

Shiba-yama Principal Confesses Inside Story of Tenko-kai Organization

Toyama Mitsuru's Son Arrested in Connection with the Inukai Assassination Case

Tokyo, 5th (Reuters) - Police raided the home of anti-reactionary leader Toyama Mitsuru and one of his organizations this morning, discovering a major conspiracy. Several people have been arrested, including Toyama Mitsuru's third son, Toyama Hidezo. Toyama Mitsuru has great influence and is highly respected by ardent patriots, so the authorities have not dared to infringe upon him lightly.

Tokyo, 5th (Denstu) - The Metropolitan Police Department, in conjunction with the Procuratorate, has been unusually tense for several days due to the autumn grand maneuvers. At 5:30 AM on the 5th, Inspector Yoshioka and seven subordinates in steel armor arrested Toyama Hidezo (age 26), the leader of the Tenko-kai, Toyama Mitsuru's third son, in Asagaya, Suginami Ward, and seized numerous related documents. Meanwhile, five squads of police officers formed by the Procuratorate, together with a squad from the Metropolitan Police Department, searched Toyama Mitsuru's residence in Shibuya. The other four squads searched the residences of those involved and arrested those involved. The reason is that members of the Tenko-kai demanded that Yoshigoro Akanuma, the central figure in the gas suspicion, prepare election expenses for candidates of the Tenko-kai in the February election, threatening and extorting several thousand yen. The incident is very complicated. Shiba-yama Principal of the May 15th Incident gave six pistols to those involved, confessing that they were supplied by Hidezo, which is why the police are active. Due to his involvement in the May 15th Incident, he will be forcibly imprisoned soon on charges of murder and violation of gun and gunpowder control. Among those accused is Yoshioka Makoto, well-known as the former captain of the Waseda University cheering squad. The Tenko-kai recommends Toyama Mitsuru as its chairman, with Hidezo in charge of practical affairs, and Shibata Tokujiro, the president of Kokushikan University, as a supporter. It is a nationalistic right-wing group with students from various universities such as Meiji University, Takushoku University, and Kokushikan University, and it is supported by the Genyosha and works with the Ko Sakura Society. Toyama Hidezo, influenced by his father Mitsuru, is a young man of courage and accomplishment, not the type to engage in intimidation. Hidezo's involvement seems to be only in the ideological aspect. Police officers and prosecutors who searched the Tenko-kai headquarters on the third floor of the Showa House and the residences of the Yawata Club seized three pistols and numerous important documents.

Tokyo, 5th (Reuters) - After raiding Toyama Mitsuru's Tenko-kai this morning and arresting Toyama Mitsuru's third son and three other members, six members of the Independent Youth Association were also arrested. It is said that these six people are involved in a plot to destroy the Tokyo Electric Power Company and plunge the city into darkness and to assassinate certain important figures. It is now believed that the two organizations are cooperating on this plot. However, the detention of Toyama Mitsuru's comrades is clearly still related to the extortion case.

Lytton Will Speak to Members of Parliament on the Political Situation in China

London, 5th (Reuters) - Lord Lytton will speak to the Conservative Party Foreign Affairs Committee of the House of Commons on November 9th. The committee's China Subcommittee will be chaired by Earl Winterton on that day. It is heard that members of Parliament familiar with Far Eastern affairs are paying close attention to the section of the Lytton Report that states that the political instability of China is the root of all troubles. It is expected that Lord Lytton's speech will focus on this point.

Special Article

The League of Nations Special Conference and the Japanese-American War (Continued)

(Written by Japanese Navy Lieutenant Commander Tōta Ishimaru, translated by this newspaper)

Mandated Territory Issue

If Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, what will happen to the mandated territories in the South Pacific? Could this be a cause of war? Further details will be provided in a separate article. Here, I will only state my conclusion: legally speaking, these mandated territories should be interpreted as not belonging to the League of Nations but to the five major powers of Japan, Britain, the United States, France, and Italy. However, in international politics, political considerations are often necessary, and legal considerations have little power. Therefore, although Japan relies on legal theories as a backing to oppose the return of these territories, if foreign countries oppose it, especially if the United States opposes it, the outcome will become a matter of strength. Unresolved disputes over this issue could lead to war.

However, this does not mean that Japan will withdraw from the League of Nations and then war will be triggered by this issue alone. This issue will only further fuel the already dangerous atmosphere towards Japan in the League of Nations and the United States. It must be combined with the anti-Japanese pressure policies mentioned in the second and third sections below to become a supplementary mechanism to promote war.

China's Retaliation Against Japan

As mentioned above, the direct results of this League of Nations Special Conference do not seem to pose a risk of triggering war. However, what we should be wary of is the change in the League of Nations situation after the League of Nations Special Conference is held. If the Chinese side allows Japan to negotiate directly and shows a willingness to make major concessions during direct negotiations, and if the United States changes its anti-Japanese Eastern policy and adopts a pro-Japanese policy, then war can be avoided. What good fortune that would be! If not, and China resolutely retaliates against Japan, and the United States continues its current attitude, then, unless other major events suddenly erupt, war will break out around 1935.

The worst-case scenario for Japan resulting from this League of Nations Special Conference is when China refuses direct negotiations, or even if negotiations are allowed, China is unwilling to make any concessions. At this time, direct negotiations have ended in failure, and China has decided to resort to retaliatory measures against Japan.

For example, using large-scale policies to disrupt Manchuria and a large-scale economic boycott of Japan are all extremely severe retaliatory measures. The former will leave Japan with no other option but to send troops into China, occupy key locations such as Peiping and Tianjin, and continue to occupy them so that China will not dare to have any further intention of disrupting Manchuria. Then the problem will transform and become even more serious, repeating the Shanghai Incident, leading to the intervention of other countries. When the Shanghai Incident was at its most intense, how acutely sensitive were the nerves of various countries? We Japanese should still remember it clearly. If second and third Shanghai Incidents follow one after another, corresponding to the first occupation of Peiping and Tianjin, with the Japanese army occupying many important locations in mainland China, can other countries sit idly by? Then the prelude to a world war will be about to begin immediately.

Some commentators in our country have said that China, having learned its lesson from the Shanghai Incident, will not dare to create a second Shanghai Incident and bring trouble on itself. However, from China's perspective, if it can involve various countries in the Sino-Japanese war, China can use foreign hands to repel Japan. Therefore, the optimistic theory of some people has lost its value and is not worth taking.

Nine-Power Treaty Conference and Four-Power Treaty Conference

If this League of Nations Special Conference does not use any sanctions against Japan, or if it uses sanctions based on the League of Nations Covenant and Hoover-style sanctions but they are ineffective, then the United States will continue its current policy toward Japan and seek the second stage of its anti-Japanese pressure policy. Especially if China takes retaliatory measures and the situation in the Far East becomes increasingly bad, calm American public opinion will also become heated, and it will inevitably support its government's second stage of anti-Japanese pressure policy. At this time, the US government will finally have the opportunity to take a proactive stance.

The so-called second stage of policies to pressure Japan will not go beyond the following two: (1) convening a Nine-Power Treaty Conference on China, and (2) convening a Four-Power Treaty Conference on the Pacific. The original intention of the United States in convening these conferences was to use these conferences to solidify the bond between Britain, the United States, and France and to jointly restrain Japan. However, if there is a proposal to convene such a conference, Japan can resolutely refuse to participate, needless to say. Because, from a legal perspective, according to Article 7 of the Nine-Power Treaty and Article 2 of the Four-Power Treaty, the contracting countries can only notify and negotiate. Countries that receive a notice from the United States are not obligated to agree to the US measures. For this reason, even if our country puts the received notice on the shelf, it will not violate the treaty at all.

If Japan refuses to participate, the convening of the conference will ultimately fail. The result will only make US-Japan relations increasingly worse, and the danger of war will lurk within it.

The 1935 Disarmament Conference

If the convening notices for the Four-Power Treaty and Nine-Power Treaty conferences are rejected, the only recourse for the United States is to wait for the 1935 Disarmament Conference.

The naval limitations and Pacific defense limitations stipulated by the Washington and London Naval Treaties will expire at the end of 1936. The conference to create a new disarmament treaty to replace these treaties should be convened in 1935. I believe that the United States will use this conference to try to exert final pressure on Japan. Naval arms reduction is certainly on the agenda, but the Manchurian issue will also be specifically raised and a settlement requested. What kind of disarmament proposal the United States will put forward at that time can be roughly gleaned from the Hoover disarmament proposal recently submitted to the League of Nations. This disarmament proposal was not established in the League of Nations because it focused on opposing Britain and Japan. However, now that Britain has expressed a willingness to compromise, this Hoover disarmament proposal will be the most important topic at the 1935 Disarmament Conference, and the main focus of this disarmament proposal is to completely block Japan's naval power.

Regarding the Manchurian issue, the United States will cite Japan's precedents in Shandong and Siberia and use the aforementioned Hoover-style sanctions as a shield to demand that Japan return Manchuria to China or impose minimal restrictions on Japan's interests in Manchuria.

Page 9

Continued from Special Article

Since Japan already knows that the United States harbors such intentions, it is not impossible for Japan to refuse to participate in the 1935 Disarmament Conference altogether. If this is the case, the United States, on the one hand, will declare that Japan has refused to participate in a peace conference, and on the other hand, since the Washington and London Treaties will expire at the end of 1936, - according to the treaty provisions, the notice of abandonment should be given two years earlier in 1934 - it will directly move towards a large-scale expansion of its navy and do its best to complete the preparations for the Philippines and Guam, making rapid progress. Then the relationship between Japan and the United States will suddenly revert to the situation before the Washington Conference, and the opening of the war will be approaching moment by moment. At that time, Britain will also be forced to follow the United States and be drawn into the vortex of the Japanese-American war. The result may trigger a Second World War. This whole armed conflict will start with the Manchurian Incident, the Pacific War between Japan, Britain, and the United States will be staged in the middle, and the Second World War will be the finale. It is truly a war chain drama. The tragedy and horror of the scene will be a hundred or a thousand times greater than that of Manchuria and Shanghai. How could the original instigator have dreamed of this?

Since I have already seen the worsening of the situation and no matter what methods are used, except for returning Manchuria, war cannot be avoided, then delaying the time will only increase the disadvantage for Japan, needless to say. Moreover, in terms of the ratio of naval power and the state of the economy, Japan is better off fighting a quick war. Then, rather than waiting until after 1936 and waiting for others to attack me, wouldn't it be better to strike first before 1936? This is why I have the outrageous argument that the sooner the war starts, the better.

The Path Japan Should Take

If this League of Nations Special Conference takes the most dangerous path in dealing with Japan, then Japan should move forward courageously with the determination to fight a war and fulfill its original purpose.

Conversely, if the current situation is relatively favorable to us, then Japan must also greatly change its policy and show the world the utmost sincerity of peace-loving. Only then will it not lose its position as a wise nation-builder. Other things, such as advocating militarism and allowing soldiers to be restless and presumptuously try to influence national policy, will ultimately bring disaster to the country, no matter what the circumstances. It is difficult to guarantee that the tragedy of Germany will not be repeated. We must repeatedly reflect on this.

Japan is now standing at a crucial fork in the road between war and peace. It must not be constrained by narrow local views and traditional xenophobic ideas. It must focus on the general trend of the world to manage national affairs, so as to win the final victory. This is also what I earnestly hope for from our government and our people.

Important News

Japan Feels Northern Manchuria is Tricky

Unable to Cope with Su Bingwen's Army

Special Dispatch from Beiping: Yesterday, I received a letter dated the 28th from a friend in Harbin, stating that Japan believed that the Northeast Three Provinces would be theirs without much effort. They thought that as long as the Japanese army arrived and there were a few Chinese traitors to act as internal collaborators, there would be no problem. They could shape it however they wanted and arrange it as they pleased. Moreover, they considered that they had been operating in Southern Manchuria for over twenty years, and not only did they have military power to control everything, but they also controlled the economic power, mostly under the guidance of the Japanese government and military. Therefore, they assumed that annexing the Northeast Three Provinces would be very convenient. However, after the September 18th Incident, the annexation policy has been tested for a year, with many tricks played, from the Public Security Maintenance Association to the puppet government, and through many tools used by Japan. Now, even ordinary Japanese adventurers are personally taking office in the puppet state, but the general situation has not improved, and there is no hope of improvement. Even the minimum level of security cannot be maintained. The South Manchuria Railway, which used to be the safest and best-managed railway, is now almost avoided by everyone. Even those who must travel by train are extremely cautious, because along the route, there is a disturbance almost every day or even every hour. Robberies and battles were once things that Japanese newspapers and local authorities paid close attention to, with monthly statistics. Railway disruptions or delays were considered emergencies. Now, people are almost used to it. Japanese authorities, for the sake of appearances, have banned newspapers from publishing news about traffic disruptions, but the general public still pays close attention to this matter, and the resentment towards the Japanese is deepening day by day. Many people who were previously dissatisfied with the Zhang regime and had pro-Japanese sentiments now realize their past mistakes, and the flames of national sentiment are reigniting. Therefore, many troops in the puppet state have different intentions. The Japanese army still places them on the front lines, using machine guns to supervise them from behind, but defections still happen every day. The vast wilderness of the Northeast provides ample space for such activities.

In Southern Manchuria, transportation is relatively convenient, making it easy for the Japanese to transport supplies and mobilize reinforcements. Therefore, large-scale volunteer armies cannot easily gain a foothold. However, the situation is different in the north, especially with the recent uprisings of Su Bingwen and Zhang Dianjiu's armies, which are most interesting. For over a month now, the Japanese army in the area from Harbin to Qiqihar includes the entire Himeji 10th Division, approximately 20,000 troops, along with other special units. The total number of Japanese troops north of Changchun exceeds 30,000, but they dare not attack Su's forces (the National Salvation Volunteer Army).

The reason why they dare not attack, according to the Japanese themselves, is that over two hundred Japanese soldiers are imprisoned in the Hailar-Manzhouli area, and over three hundred Japanese women and children are being held there. If the Japanese army launches an attack, these hundreds of people will lose their lives. Therefore, they must first rescue the detained people before using force. In reality, the reasons for not using force are: first, the Japanese army itself is already tired of fighting for the merit of warlords; second, the Northeast region is too vast, and a small number of troops cannot easily defend it. If a large number of troops are mobilized, it would cost a huge amount of military expenses with little gain; third, the Chinese Eastern Railway has relations with the Soviet Union, and using force along the Chinese Eastern Railway would provoke unexpected disputes at a time when Japan is seeking to maintain good relations with the Soviet Union. Moreover, the commander of the Soviet Far East Army is pro-war, so how can Japan not be concerned? Therefore, Japan can only talk about peace with the volunteer army in the western section of the Chinese Eastern Railway and even invite the Soviet consul to help rescue the detained Japanese. The front line of the Japanese army is in Gannan, and there is no sign of advancing westward. Their demands on Su are:

1. Immediately cease the anti-Manchu and anti-Japanese attitude.

2. Withdraw the troops along the railway and return to the original defense, without hindering traffic.

3. Appoint Su Bingwen as the commander of the Hulunbuir Garrison.

4. Supply the Su army with military expenses of 200,000 yuan.

5. Immediately and unconditionally release the detained Japanese.

Unexpectedly, Su did not budge and continued to actively prepare, with Deputy Commander Zhang Dianjiu as the vanguard. They also established a government in Hailar, and their front-line troops, in the Zhu Jiakan-Nianzishan area, built trenches to prepare for battle. They also detained two Japanese reconnaissance planes and five crew members, including Major Watanabe. The Japanese military and political authorities in Longjiang and Harbin are very anxious and have sent two bombers and one fighter plane to carry out intimidation, but none of them have returned. It is said that they were all shot down. On the night of October 27, about 500 volunteer soldiers launched a night attack on Longjiang, fighting until dawn, and then retreated due to being outnumbered. The volunteer army is very mysterious, so the Japanese are very wary of the Chinese in Harbin, especially those from inland, fearing that we will respond to the volunteer army.

Sudden Changes in Sichuan Situation

Liu Wenhui and Deng Xihou Establish New Understanding

Chengdu Conference to Negotiate Ceasefire Terms

Liu Xiang Goes to the Front, Dividing into Three Routes to Attack Luzhou and Neijiang

Correspondent from Hankou: The internal war in Sichuan Province, caused by the rivalry between Liu Wenhui and Liu Xiang for supremacy, has been fueled by neutral generals who are adding fuel to the fire in order to reap the benefits. For the past month, in addition to the clashes between the two armies, there have been alliances to overthrow Liu (Wenhui), proposals to break up defense zones, the initiation of the Suining Conference, and the implementation of armed mediation. All kinds of strategies and intrigues can be described as extremely volatile. Until recently, the inside story of this false alliance has gradually been revealed, and the Sichuan situation has suddenly changed. At the beginning of the conflict between the two Lius, Liu Wenhui's strength was superior to Liu Xiang's. Liu Xiang sent representatives everywhere to win over Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao, Liu Cunhou, and Yang Sen, advocating the theory of an alliance to help himself. Deng, Tian, Liu, and Yang, knowing there were benefits to be gained, readily agreed. However, when the war broke out, the only troops engaged in combat were the direct subordinates of the two Lius, Luo Zezhou and Li Jiayu, while Deng, Tian, Liu, and Yang remained on the sidelines. Liu Xiang, now in a predicament, had to fully attack, wanting to resolve the 24th Army in one fell swoop, and then slowly deal with Deng, Tian, Liu, and Yang. Although he still outwardly promoted the alliance, in reality, they were already at odds. Liu Wenhui saw through his intention and tried his best to befriend Deng and Tian, promising to cede Ziyang and Jianyang counties to Deng and Tian's troops for defense. Deng and Tian, both from the Baoding Military Academy, had always been allies, and many of their subordinates, division and brigade commanders, were also graduates of Baoding. They had an inseparable relationship. Although Liu, Deng, and Tian had recent disagreements, they were not deep-seated enemies. Once the misunderstanding was cleared, they could resolve their grievances and become friends. Therefore, after receiving Ziyang and Jianyang, Deng and Tian's attitude changed immediately. They have now established a new understanding with Liu Wenhui and negotiated ceasefire terms, calling for the Chengdu Conference. Yang Sen, secluded in a corner, having already sent troops, wanted to get a share of the pie to increase his defense area, so he is also brewing to join. Liu Cunhou, the oldest of all the generals, had both Lius as his subordinates. Liu Wenhui is willing to divide the land among Deng, Tian, and Yang, and would certainly not leave out this old man. In this situation, Liu Xiang, who sees himself as the leader of the alliance, has been forced into isolation. However, although Liu Xiang knows the situation is precarious, he is not willing to submit. In recent days, he has continuously mobilized his troops, dividing them into three routes to advance towards Luzhou and Neijiang. On the third day, he went to the Yonglu front to慰劳his troops and encourage a fierce attack. At the same time, he has also been vigorously publicizing victories to boost his prestige. Yesterday, on the third day, another telegram of victory arrived in Hankou, disclosed below: 1. The enemy in Longchang retreated in large numbers towards Neijiang on the afternoon of the Eastern day, and a small number retreated towards Niu Fu Du. Our army is in pursuit. 2. Our army's units of Yang, Li, Luo, and Zeng arrived in Anyue on the 31st to await orders. 3. Deng's unit telegraphed that they have received Chen Shuhong's unit, but Chen Hongwen's unit needs to wait a little longer due to environmental reasons before they can return. 4. Deng led a part of his troops out of Ziyang and Jianyang to receive Chen Hongwen's troops and to block the enemy's retreat. General Tian will lead the majority of his troops to help Deng open the eastern route to complete the second phase of operations. 5. Taking Ziyang and Luzhou is just around the corner. 6. Suppression of Communists to Shift Focus to Borders of Jiangxi, Zhejiang and Fujian

After remnants of Zhu De and Mao Zedong's bandit forces infiltrated Northern Fujian

They colluded with bandit gangs led by Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping in Northeastern Jiangxi

Recapturing bandit lairs in Southern Jiangxi will not be a problem

The most difficult issues are post-conflict management and self-defense

Nanchang dispatch: Zhu De, Mao Zedong, and Peng Dehuai failed in their northern invasion of Yihuang and Le'an, and after fleeing back to Ningdu and Xingguo, Guo Bingsheng, the commander of their so-called Second Division, surrendered to the National Revolutionary Army. The National Revolutionary Army jointly blockaded the communist areas and their so-called Soviet areas, such as Xunwu, Huichang, Ruijin, Yudu, Xingguo, Shicheng, Guangchang in Southeastern Jiangxi, and Yongfeng, Jishui, Ji'an, Le'an and other southern areas. For years, these places had been drained of resources, and it was difficult to sustain the communist presence there. Therefore, Zhu De and Mao Zedong convened a so-called Central Conference in Ningdu, where the following decisions were made: 1) To greatly reduce and reorganize the Red Army; 2) Before Chiang Kai-shek and his main forces arrive in Jiangxi, to launch a large-scale invasion of Northern Fujian to find supplies and establish new bases to break the economic blockade. After this decision, Zhu De and Xiang Ying, in the name of the puppet Military Commission, reduced the original five army corps to three. Lin Biao was the commander of the so-called First Army Corps, commanding the Second and Fourth Armies. Peng Dehuai commanded the so-called Third Army Corps, commanding the Fifth and Seventh Armies. Luo Binghui commanded the so-called Fifth Army Corps (some say Dong Zhentang held the position of commander, but the original commander was Ji Zhendong, a traitor under Sun Lianzhong, who has been confirmed to have been killed), commanding the Thirteenth, Fourteenth, and Fifteenth Armies. All other units that were not full-fledged armies were reorganized into independent regiments and independent divisions. Luo Binghui's so-called Twenty-second Army remained directly under Zhu De's command. After the reorganization of the bandit army, funds were lacking. The official rations for the Red Army were 13 cents per day, while miscellaneous troops, such as independent divisions and guerrillas, received 6 cents per day. In reality, they were owed for months, and even a few copper coins for daily vegetables could not be paid. With nothing left to rob or search, the communist bandits were forced to urgently infiltrate Fujian. Before mid-last month, Zhu De and Mao Zedong concentrated their main forces in the Shicheng, Ninghua, and Guangchang areas, and invaded Northern Fujian in three routes. The central route, led by Lin Biao, directly invaded Jianning and Jiangle. The right route, led by Luo Binghui, attacked Ningdu and Shaowu. The left route, led by Peng Dehuai and Sheng Daiyuan, attacked Lichuan (which has since been recovered) and Guangze. The so-called headquarters of the Third Army Corps was stationed in Kangdeng, at the border of Lichuan, Nanfeng, Guangchang, Jianning, and Taining. Their mission was to protect the Jiangxi border to defend against attacks from the National Revolutionary Army in Nancheng and Nanfeng, with no intention of occupying Lichuan for long. Therefore, the so-called Fifth and Third Armies, and the Twenty-first Division, after plundering Lichuan dry, withdrew, intending to lure the National Revolutionary Army into the communist area of Guangchang for battle. At that time, Li Yunjie, Mao Bingwen, and Pang Kexiang had strong fortifications near the Fujian border in Nancheng and Nanfeng, adopting only a defensive posture and not pursuing the bandits. According to recent news from the front, the communist bandits, realizing that it was difficult to survive in isolation, mostly reorganized into smaller units. For example, Kuang Jixun merged with He Duan, and Kong Helong merged with the so-called Eighth Army in Western Jiangxi. Lin Biao and Luo Binghui, after occupying Jianning and Taining, actively expanded northward through Jiangle, Shaowu, and Guangze, hoping to join forces with Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping on the border of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui, concentrating their forces to expand the communist area and consolidate the Jiangxi-Zhejiang-Fujian border front. After being besieged by the five divisions of Zhou Jinyuan, Wang Jinwen, Zhao Guantao, Li Yunhan, and Ruan Zhaochang, Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping's original bandit lairs, such as Geyuan and Jufang, were completely destroyed. The so-called organs and all equipment were swept away, and the Soviet areas on both sides of the Xin River were blockaded by Jiangxi and Zhejiang, with no way in or out. They could not plunder food from the nearby guerrilla areas, so they had to find another way out. Therefore, the gang recently left Shao Shiping to guard the rear, while Fang Zhimin led the so-called Tenth Army, independent divisions, guard divisions, and others, totaling several thousand people, back into Chong'an, Jianyang, and Guangze from Guangfeng and Qianshan to join Luo Binghui's forces in Taining and Shaowu. According to captured bandits, the two gangs have already colluded. Zhu De and Mao Zedong even sent a wireless radio to Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping as a tool for military communication. At present, the communist bandit front starts from the Jiangxi-Fujian border, passing through Xunwu, Huichang, Ruijin, Shicheng, Guangchang, Lichuan, and Western Fujian, bordering the above-mentioned counties in Jiangxi, and connecting Shanghang, Wuping, Changting, Ninghua, Jianning, Taining, Shaowu, and Guangze in the north, and extending north to Chong'an, Pucheng, Qianshan, Guangfeng, Shangrao, and Dexing on the border of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui, forming a long snake. The center of the communist bandit activity is in Jianning, where Zhu De and Mao Zedong are stationed to command. With the changes in the communist bandit situation as described above, the focus of suppressing communists has shifted from the border of Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Fujian to the border of Jiangxi, Fujian, and Zhejiang. According to military sources, Chiang Kai-shek, with the communist threat in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui already cleared, urgently needs to suppress Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Fang Zhimin, and Kong Helong's forces. He has decided to come to Jiangxi to command the campaign in person after ten days. Some of the additional troops he is sending to Jiangxi have already arrived. The supply depots of the three provinces have been established, and Yu Feipeng will come to Jiangxi within days to direct military transportation. These are all preludes to a large-scale campaign. As for the plans and arrangements for suppressing the communists, due to the need for secrecy, details will be omitted for now. According to those who escaped from Xingguo, the communist rear (Southern Jiangxi) is extremely empty. Escapees were inspected by child and female sentries, with no regular Red Army soldiers present. Production in the communist area has ceased, almost like an undeveloped deserted island or an uninhabited barren mountain. All the old and weak will starve to death. The communist bandits regard this as a bloodless and lifeless corpse. Our army can completely recover Southern Jiangxi with just one or two divisions. However, after the recovery, the troops will have no supplies, the people will not be able to defend themselves, and returning refugees will not be able to survive. Post-conflict management and self-defense are a major problem and the most difficult aspect. (November 4)

The Situation of Bandits in Northern Fujian is Severe

The Pacification Commissioner's Office is Actively Planning Suppression

Fuzhou dispatch: It is heard that before this communist bandit invasion of Northern Fujian, the bandits convened a meeting in Ruijin and formed a general labor union, electing the bandit leader Lin Biao as the puppet chairman. Fearing encirclement by the large anti-bandit force in Jiangxi and the anti-bandit forces in Guangdong and Fujian, they decided to have the bandit leader Peng Dehuai lead bandits in Huichang to harass Jiangxi, to prevent being attacked from the rear. Meanwhile, bandit leaders Zhu De and Lin Biao led their forces to infiltrate Fujian, planning to join forces with Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping's gangs in Chong'an and Pucheng, and then split up to infiltrate the Zhejiang border, forming a base on the border of Zhejiang, Jiangxi, and Fujian. Therefore, after Zhu De and Lin Biao led Luo Binghui and other gangs into Jianning and Taining, they moved horizontally into Shaowu, and then split into two routes from Shaowu. One route, supervised by Zhu De, spied on Jianyang from Masha, so that they could contact Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping's gangs in Chong'an and Pucheng to enter the Zhejiang border. The other route, supervised by Lin Biao and Luo Binghui, spied on Jiangle from Shaowu, intending to enter Shunchang Yangkou to plunder silver and goods to replenish the army. Yangkou is a major town upstream, where the commercial essence of Yanping, Jianning, Shaowu, and Tingzhou converges, so it is coveted by the bandits. Now, Zhu De's gang arrived at Tabu (50 li from Jianyang) from Masha on October 24. After fierce fighting with the Zhou Brigade and Hu Regiment of the garrison for two hours, Hu retreated to Fengle Town between Jianyang and Jian'ou due to being outnumbered. The bandits then occupied Jianyang City on the 25th. After the bandits entered Jianyang, on the 27th, they sent bandits to spy on Huangyang, and another group of bandits went north to join forces with Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping's gangs, intending to enter Zhejiang. As for Lin Biao's bandit force, they looted the wealth of merchants and wealthy people in Shaowu, and seized large quantities of grain from various villages. They also sent bandits to spy on Jiangle. On the 28th, according to news from refugees fleeing Yangkou to the province, Jiangle was also occupied by the bandits on the 26th. Therefore, the defense of Shunchang is very strained. Liu's division telegraphed yesterday that defenses have been strengthened in Yangkou, Jian'ou, Nanping, and other places. The suburbs of Yanping are also rushing to build defensive fortifications. All the troops of the division stationed on the south bank of the Min River (Hongshan and above Shuikouwankou area) were transferred to Yanping yesterday to assist in defense. The defenses in various places are quite solid. After the Fuzhou Pacification Commissioner's Office received the telegram from the military authorities in Northern Fujian about the bandit situation, it has been responding with telegrams for days, giving instructions to plan the encirclement and suppression. Yesterday, the office also sent a special commissioner to Yanping and Jianning to inspect the defenses in order to be thorough. Meanwhile, the office ordered the Chen Wei Yuan's Third Provincial Brigade, which had set out for the province, to rush to garrison the Minqing area. If necessary, they would be sent from Minqing to Yanping to assist Liu's division in defense. The brigade arrived in the Da Xiao Ruo area on the 27th. Lin Bingzhou's Second Brigade of the Marine Corps also received orders from the Pacification Commissioner's Office to move from Funing to the Gutian area. The entire First Brigade of the Marine Corps was also transferred to the Changle area. All began to move yesterday. As for the Zhejiang army led by Dai Yue, which came to Fujian to assist in the suppression, it has received a telegram from He Yingqin, ordering them to move to the Fujian border. At present, to prevent the bandits from fleeing north into Zhejiang, they have begun to suppress them on the border of Fujian and Zhejiang. Zhao Guantao's division has also entered Fujian and joined forces with the garrison in Chong'an to encircle and suppress Fang Zhimin's forces, killing more than ten bandits on the spot and capturing more than one hundred rifles, cutting off the bandit's communication lines. From now on, the armies of the three provinces will join forces to suppress the bandits, and it should not be difficult to eliminate them. (October 29)

Another dispatch: Zhu De and Lin Biao led the so-called First and Third Army Corps from Eastern Jiangxi to invade Northern Fujian, successively capturing Jianning, Taining, Shaowu, and Guangze, and threatening Jiangle and Jianyang. The situation upstream is suddenly tense. Liu Heding, commander of the Fifty-sixth Division, has decided to defend Jian'ou and Shunchang with all his strength to secure Yanping. The front line of Jian'ou is in Fengle Village, at the junction of Jian'ou and Jianyang, defended by Zhou Zhimin's brigade. However, Zhou's troops suffered considerable losses in the battles of Taining and Shaowu and are awaiting replenishment. Therefore, one regiment of Ma Hongxing's troops has been added to assist them. The front line of Shunchang is in Gaotan Town, at the junction of Shunchang and Jiangle, defended by Gui Zhenyuan's brigade. Liu Heding himself went to the front in Jian'ou from Yanping a few days ago to supervise the troops and engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits in Huangyang, forcing Lin Biao's forces to retreat. The bandit forces have retreated slightly. The bandit's original plan was to have Lin Biao stationed in Taining, directing the attack on Jianyang and Jiangle, while Zhu De was stationed in Jianning, directing the attack on Guihua and Qingliu, with two routes advancing simultaneously, attempting to contain the National Revolutionary Army's advance. Now, because the National Revolutionary Army's Wang Jinwen and Mao Hongwen's divisions in Jiangxi province are advancing on Qianshan and Lichuan, approaching the Fujian border, Lin Biao, Zhu De, and other bandits fear that their rear will be cut off, and Zhu De has urgently led the so-called First Army Corps back to Guangchang and Shicheng on the Jiangxi border from Jianning and Ninghua, intending to resist. Therefore, the newly formed First Division under Lu Xingbang, stationed in Yong'an and Shaxian, immediately sent troops to take over the defense of Guihua and Qingliu. Lin Biao's forces in Taining and Shaowu were greatly affected and dared not advance further. Liu Heding telegraphed yesterday, stating that the defense of the entire line has been completed, and once the Jiangxi army enters Fujian, a large-scale counterattack can be launched to achieve a pincer attack. However, most of the refugees from Jianning, Taining, Shaowu, Guangze, and Jiangle are still gathered in Yanping Yangkou, and a small number are taking boats to the province, staying in the guild halls of their respective counties. Yesterday, the Northern Fujian Hometown Relief Association petitioned the Pacification Commissioner's Office and the Provincial Government, requesting that shelters be set up in Yangkou, Yanping, and Fuzhou to accommodate them and allocate funds for relief to avoid displacement. (November 1)

Lin Yizhong Reports on His Trip to Siam

Guangzhou dispatch: Lin Yizhong, Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Guangdong Province, departed from Hong Kong for Siam on September 19 with Xiao Focheng to congratulate the Siamese People's Party on its success. They arrived in Bangkok on the 28th. Xiao Focheng had made prior arrangements, so all entry inspection procedures were waived. After arriving in Siam, they paid visits to the President of the Senate, Yemanu, the leader of the People's Party, Cheng Paliet, the Commander-in-Chief of the National Army, the Minister of Foreign Affairs, and others. They also visited Bangkok's police agencies, prisons, palaces, hospitals, schools, and Buddhist temples. After the visit, they left Siam for Singapore on the 12th of last month and returned to Guangdong by boat. However, Xiao Focheng remained in Siam, with no news of his return. On the 31st, Lin reported on his inspection of Siam during the memorial week of the Southwest Executive Department's Political Affairs Committee. Excerpts are recorded as follows: Since the revolution in Siam, the royal family only has the power to issue decrees, and state affairs are decided by the Senate. The senior administrative agencies include the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Justice, the General Staff, and the National Army Headquarters. The country is divided into nine provinces and one capital city. Provinces have governors, and cities have mayors and a police commissioner, all under the Ministry of Interior. Provinces are divided into prefectures, prefectures are divided into counties, and counties are divided into townships, with ten households per village, ten villages per township, and ten or more townships per county. The administration and police of the capital city are separate, each with its own department. Provincial police administration is under administrative control. The military system adopts conscription, and men are required to serve three years of military service upon reaching the age of eighteen. Public security is the responsibility of the police, and the National Army is responsible for national defense. There are about 2 million overseas Chinese in Siam, most of whom are engaged in business. Among the overseas Chinese, the largest number are from Chaozhou and Guangzhou, followed by people from Hainan and Fujian. People from Guangzhou are in the minority. The largest overseas Chinese business is the rice industry, followed by lumber mills. The rest are coolies, farmers, or land reclaimers. China and Siam do not have a treaty, and although overseas Chinese in Siam do not have consular protection, they are not treated harshly because of similarities in skin color and race. Overseas Chinese only need to pay an entry tax of 40 yuan per person to enter Siam. Overseas Chinese in Siam can freely operate businesses and buy and sell land, but gatherings and associations for political patriotic activities are strictly prohibited. Twenty years ago, Siam had no overseas Chinese schools, and overseas Chinese children mostly attended Siamese schools, where they were assimilated and had weak patriotic ideas. After the establishment of overseas Chinese schools, the children of overseas Chinese were able to recognize Chinese characters and learn about the concept of the motherland. Currently, there are only 12 overseas Chinese primary schools in Bangkok, so many overseas Chinese are still illiterate. Overseas Chinese are all in the industrial and commercial sectors and do not have a clear understanding of the politics of their motherland, relying only on local Chinese newspapers for information. Although there are four Chinese newspaper offices in the area, they each have their own backgrounds and it is difficult to get accurate news from China. However, although overseas Chinese sometimes misunderstand the politics of their motherland, their concern remains strong. During the Shanghai Incident, they donated 5-600,000 yuan to support the anti-Japanese national salvation effort. Their only hope is that their motherland will no longer have civil wars and will concentrate the nation's strength to resist foreign aggression. (November 1)

Guangdong Province Establishes Publication Review Committee

Jointly organized by party and government agencies

Regulations on Review of Publications Have Been Promulgated

Guangzhou dispatch: Guangdong Province is recently preparing a highest level Publication Review Committee, to carry out reviews on various publications published locally, in order to stop communist propaganda and the dissemination of all reactionary publications. This committee can be established within one week. The Publication Review Committee is organized jointly by the Southwest Executive Department, the Guangdong Provincial Party Headquarters, the Guangzhou Special Municipal Party Headquarters, the Guangdong Provincial Public Security Bureau, and the Guangzhou Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. It will have eleven standing directors, with three senior personnel sent by the Southwest Executive Department and the provincial and municipal party headquarters respectively, and one person in charge sent by the Public Security Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau respectively, forming a standing directors office. The standing directors office will set up a number of inspectors, appointed by the standing directors office from the propaganda personnel of party headquarters at all levels, or other personnel as adjuncts. The area for review is temporarily limited to Guangzhou City, and will be expanded as necessary. As for the temporary regulations on review, they were issued by the Southwest Executive Department yesterday and are appended below: 1) In order to prevent reactionary propaganda, the party headquarters at all levels in the Southwest may review all publications published or circulated in the Southwest, in accordance with the provisions of these regulations. The reactionary publications referred to in these regulations are all those that violate Articles 19, Paragraph 1 to Paragraph 4 of the Publication Law. 2) In order to ensure thorough review and rapidly prevent reactionary publications, party headquarters at the provincial level or party headquarters at the same level as the province may jointly establish a publication review committee with local agencies. 3) The detailed rules for the organization of the publication review committee may be stipulated in consideration of local conditions, but must be reported to the Southwest Executive Department for approval and record. 4) If the party headquarters of each county and city finds reactionary publications, it should report to the review committee of the province and city, or to the higher-level party headquarters, to discuss with the local government to ban it. 5) The publications of all groups or individuals must be submitted by the publisher or distributor to the local publication review committee at the time of publication or when they arrive at the place of sale. They may only be sold after the review is permitted. 6) If the publication review committee considers that a publication has reactionary properties, it should report it to the local highest party headquarters, and should first consult with the local government to prohibit its sale and distribution, and may detain it when necessary. 7) All printing shops in various places must not undertake the printing of reactionary publications. Whenever they encounter books, leaflets, or slogans related to politics for printing, if there is no responsible person from the local party headquarters or government agency, and it has not been reviewed and approved by the publication review committee, they must immediately submit the original to the local publication review committee for review. Whoever violates the provisions of these regulations, publishes, sells, distributes, or prints reactionary publications privately, will be reported by the publication review committee to the local highest party headquarters and forwarded to the local government, who will give warnings, seals, or penalties in accordance with the provisions of the Publication Law, depending on the circumstances. 8) These temporary regulations will be implemented from the date of promulgation. (October 29)

Profound Dissertation after the Investigation of Northeastern China by Westerners (Continued)

2. Harbin and Changchun Area: Due to this year's floods and the activities of the Volunteer Army, the supply of food is extremely difficult. The eastern and western sections of the Chinese Eastern Railway cannot be used for transportation because the two sections of the railway are almost completely under the control of the Volunteer Army. Therefore, the value of various foods is extremely high, and postal communication is often interrupted. For example, letters from Shenyang to Harbin sometimes take ten days. Yagi, the Japanese advisor in the Harbin Police Department, has reorganized the police personnel in Harbin, but the result has only allowed the opportunity for riots in the port to expand. The newly appointed police do not restrict rioters, so the citizens of the entire port are in a state of panic. The Soviet employees of the Chinese Eastern Railway were previously slacking off, but now they are working completely according to Japanese wishes. In Changchun City (Yamatodaei), important streets have evicted local residents from their residences because the puppet government needs 700 houses for the residence of puppet government officials. Since August, construction work has been expanded in Changchun and Kuanchengzi, and workers have been ordered to work day and night. There is also a feeling of a lack of stone needed for construction. In Harbin, Changchun, Shenyang, etc., people who work against the puppet government are often arrested, but this has not improved the situation. In Shenyang, four suspects were arrested for plotting to harm Saitō (October 6), one of whom was a White Russian immigrant, Aniseff. Leaflets in Chinese denouncing the puppet government and expelling the Japanese are often found in the above-mentioned areas.

The Ministry of Education of the Manchukuo puppet government has been in arrears with the salaries of teachers in various schools since the beginning of this year. The teachers' salaries for January were paid in three installments: 20% was paid in February, 30% in March, and 50% in April. The salaries for February were paid in two installments: 50% was paid in May and 50% in June. The salaries for March were only paid 50% at the end of July, and it was announced that the remaining 50% would be suspended. After that, 50% of the teachers' salaries for April were paid in August. According to information received, all personnel in the Ministry of Education of Manchukuo are actively carrying out anti-Japanese and anti-Manchu work, providing assistance to the Chinese Volunteer Army. The teachers in various schools are also voluntarily donating part of their salaries to the anti-Japanese movement and carrying out extensive anti-Japanese propaganda among the students in the schools. This kind of action is supported by teachers. In short, all civil servants in the Manchukuo puppet government are expanding their anti-Japanese and anti-Manchu thoughts. They consider their duties in the "New Country" to be like being in a period of captivity. The Japanese advisors in "Manchukuo" have already been aware of this will of the civil servants, but there is no way to improve the situation, because there are very few people who cooperate with Japan, and in order to fill the number of positions in the puppet government, it is necessary to use people with anti-Japanese thoughts. The Japanese poor who have lived in Manchuria for a long time all deny that their position in Manchuria can be consolidated. (To be continued)

Important News Two

Zhenjiang Port Plan

Due to changes in the canal transport route, the opening of the Jinpu Railway, and the increasing siltation of sandbars in the river, Zhenjiang's commerce and industry have been declining. After the provincial government moved to Zhenjiang, the authorities, in order to develop industry and commerce and promote the prosperity of the port, proposed building a new port at Xiangshan. The Construction Department is now actively working to make it a reality. It is heard that the latest plan is to make river management the foundation for building a new port. If the river does not follow the right course, it is difficult to guarantee that the newly built port will not repeat past mistakes. In order to get to the root of the problem, it is planned to start by correcting the waterways upstream and downstream of Zhenjiang. The north and south waterways of Shiyezhou and the Zhengrunzhou waterway must be improved first, and the surface of the island must be raised. The Liuyu area on the north bank will be subject to bank protection and construction projects. Then, Zhengrunzhou, with an area of 15,000 mu, will be converted into a commercial port. The construction plan for the Xiangshan New Port is divided into public wharf and commercial area. The wharf will have four lighters to accommodate river ships. There is a canal located south of the warehouses, 920 meters long, for small boats and sailboats to dock. There is a boat pond located in the eastern part of the area, 400 meters long, connected to the canal and the Yangtze River, for civilian boats to dock temporarily in case of wind and also for repairing boats and sailboats. There are spacious warehouses to meet the needs of cargo storage. The commercial area is located west of the boat pond and south of the canal, with a total area of more than 12,000 acres together with the public wharf area. It is connected to the city and West Gate Street by three trunk lines. The railway is particularly important. It is planned to build a branch line from the Zhenjiang South Gate Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, crossing the canal and reaching the wharf directly, so that the waterway and railway can be connected, making the transportation of goods and the traffic of merchants more convenient. In addition, the roads will be paved with crushed stone, with widths divided into five grades, the widest being 24 meters and the narrowest being 10 meters, divided into three major trunk lines, so that the new and old urban areas can be connected everywhere.

Local News

Wuxi

The Embezzlement of the Accountant of the Charity Hall is Exposed

Tongren Nursery and Yuying Hall in Xinmiaoqian, in the city

The Tongren Nursery and Yuying Hall, established by the Qin and Hua families, have a long history. The Tongren Hall has more than a thousand acres of farmland, and the collected rent is allocated for charity purposes. Hua Zhongyuan, the accountant of the two halls, has been in charge since he took office in the 16th year of the Republic of China, monopolizing power and keeping the accounts secret and not making them public. Recently, the board of directors found that Hua Zhongyuan had inflated expenses and embezzled a total of 15,000 yuan. Therefore, the board of directors immediately issued a notice to suspend his duties, and the accounting affairs were temporarily handled by Ding Ruichu, while the accounts were being cleared. Since his suspension, Hua has been hiding in his residence at No. 1 Jinshifang Lane nearby and could not be found. Hua has instead sent a letter to a director of the board of directors, repeatedly asking Hua to seek three conditions. First, the embezzlement part will not be investigated in depth. Second, the receipts have been lost and will not be reissued. Third, the accounts can only be secretly viewed by certain two people and must not be announced to the outside world. After receiving the letter, the association submitted a request to the county court yesterday, requesting an order to bring Hua Zhongyuan to court to pursue the recovery of the embezzled funds, and a joint submission from a public group and people from all walks of life to the competent authority, requesting that Hua Zhongyuan be punished as he deserves and ordered to hand over the embezzled funds in full within a limited time.

Planned Widening of Sanxia Tang Street

Widening of Sanxia Tang Street

The case of widening Sanxia Tang Street has been repeatedly handled by the former Construction Bureau Director Yao Dixin, who sent personnel to measure and draw diagrams. Ultimately, due to the opposition of a few local residents, the project was delayed and not implemented. After Director Xiao of the Construction Bureau took office, he convened relevant representatives for a meeting and followed the Construction Department's approval to set the street standard at eight meters. This includes six meters for the carriageway, one meter on each side for sidewalks, and engineering works for road surfaces, ditches, and bridges, which are currently under design. However, the construction funding is currently unavailable, which is deeply concerning. Director Xiao will submit a detailed report on the fundraising situation to the Construction Department, along with a complete plan of Sanxia Tang Street, requesting instructions. Director Dong, after reviewing the report, stated that the primary questions are whether the street is a direct north-south thoroughfare, whether there is a need to gradually reduce the width, and whether the required construction funds can be raised. Yesterday, he specifically ordered Magistrate Chen to supervise Director Xiao of the Construction Bureau to devise a proper plan and submit it to a meeting for discussion and approval. After receiving the order, Magistrate Chen immediately instructed Director Xiao of the Construction Bureau to comply.

A Sailing Boat Robbed En Route at Panjia Bridge

A sailing boat from the Panjia Bridge area of Wuyi was robbed on the afternoon of the third. It departed from Pan Town at 4:00 PM, and while sailing between Tianjing Bridge and Daixi Bridge, it was suddenly encountered by a pirate ship containing several armed bandits. The bandits immediately boarded the sailing boat and robbed the passengers in the cabins, sparing none. Clothing and cash were stolen to a great extent, and the boat owner was pushed into the river by the bandits. Their whereabouts are currently unknown.

The inspectors sealed them up and awaited inspection and handling by the authorities.

Jiading

The Truth Comes Out in the Rural Teachers' Slogan Case

The Sixth District Security Corps arrested students for posting reactionary slogans by students from the Provincial Huangdu Rural Normal School. Initially, opinions varied. Now, after investigation by the Qingpu County Party Department, the seal of the Rural Normal School Student Self-Government Association on the slogans did not match the registered seal of the department, and the handwriting was inconsistent. It was evident that someone had forged the slogans to sabotage the school and that the slogans were not written by the school's students. The county government, based on the report from the county party department's branch in the town and the report from the school principal, Teng Yangzhi, found that the two reports did not match. Shen Jinghua, the director of the Public Security Bureau, investigated and confirmed that the corps had indeed arrested students Wang Xuegui and others and detained them in the corps' office and subjected students Gu Caiyu and Xu Linshou to handcuffs and other instruments. The report was submitted to the county. Magistrate Pan, considering the corps' actions to be illegal, ordered the arrest and prosecution of the troublemaking corps members. It is also heard that the corps, realizing their impropriety, sent the corps deputy, Zhang Jinting, as a representative to the school to acknowledge and guarantee the school's future safety and dismiss the illegal corps members to settle the matter.

Jiaxing

Xu Xianghe Silver Shop Defrauded of Gold Jewelry

Yesterday morning at around 11:00 AM, a man of about thirty years old suddenly came to Xu Xianghe Silver Shop on North Main Street in Jiaxing. He placed a paper roll on the counter and asked the shop assistant to buy a gold diamond and two gold rings. The shop assistant gave him a gold diamond weighing four qian and three li and two gold rings weighing three qian and eight li to look at. After the customer received the gold jewelry, he said he would take it to show it to "them" and then walked outside. As soon as he went out the door, he ran towards Tianning Temple Street. The shop assistant chased after him and apprehended him, taking him to the Seventh Police Station. After questioning by Patrol Officer Fang, he confessed that his name was Zhang Jiliang, from Wujiang County, and he was the principal of a primary school in Maota Township, Third District of the county. This time, because there was a happy occasion at home, he needed to exchange for jewelry. He had 103 yuan, which he had placed on the counter. He claimed that he had simply taken the jewelry to show his family to see if they liked it and did not intend to run away. Patrol Officer Fang sent the person and the evidence to the local branch court for interrogation through the County Public Security Bureau and then ordered him to be detained pending investigation. The Finance Department Assigned a Commissioner to Guard and Withdraw Taxes

Ningbo

Robbery of a Newlywed Home Leads to the Death of a Young Child

Huang Zhiqiong, a resident of Huangbian, near the Miao Bian area of Shiqi in southern Yin County, held a wedding for his son the other day. Relatives and friends gathered, and guests filled the house. Unexpectedly, at around 1:00 AM that night, after the bride and groom had already entered the bridal chamber and fallen asleep, and the guests were still playing mahjong, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived and robbed at will. No one among the male and female guests was spared. The bandits then rushed into the bridal chamber and dragged the bride and groom out of bed, taking the bride's floral jacket and gold jewelry. During the robbery, one of the bandits fired a shot to intimidate, and the bullet hit Zhi Xiang, the four-year-old son of his relative Huang Acai, killing him on the spot. The bandits then fled with a roar. The loss is estimated to be over a thousand yuan.

Important News

Jiangsu Province Boy Scouts

| Grand Jamboree Day Two |

Group Leaders Jointly Take Oath

Discipline Storytelling Speech Competition

Rehearsal for Inspection Held in the Afternoon

| Inspection Ceremony Held This Morning |

The 5th was the second day of the joint grand jamboree for Boy Scouts in secondary schools throughout Jiangsu Province, held in Zhenjiang. In the morning, various groups completed the construction of camp sites.

Camp Commander Convenes for Instructions

First, Camp Commander Chen Bangcai convened all group leaders for a talk at 7:00 AM yesterday (the 5th). The main points were as follows: 1) Group leaders must report leave to the camp administrator. 2) The material for the drill should be slightly modified. 3) The flags of each group must be raised and lowered at the same time, not earlier or later. He also convened the camp police for instructions, warning each police officer to double the punishment for those who do not obey the rules.

Holding Oath-Taking Ceremony for Group Leaders

At 8:00 AM, an oath-taking ceremony for group leaders was held. More than fifty group leaders and deputy group leaders attended. Director Zhou Fo hai of the Education Department served as the oath supervisor and delivered a speech, which stated: 1) Boy Scout training should not only be about neat uniforms and winning competitions, but also about paying attention to the usual mental training. 2) I have seen Boy Scouts in Shanghai used as decoration for funerals and weddings, which shows a fundamental misunderstanding of Boy Scout training. All those who hold the position of group leader must correct this point. 3) The mission of training Boy Scouts for all group leaders is very important, then all group leaders should be fully prepared for their own cultivation, especially do not forget that Boy Scout training is based on the realization of the Three People's Principles.

Appraisers Zhang Jun and Others Arrive in Zhenjiang

Zhang Zhongren, the chief judge of the conference, and judge Zhang Jun arrived in Zhenjiang the night before. Yesterday, judges Hu Chang and Zhou Boping also arrived in Zhenjiang. Liu Zao, the inventor of flag language, was hired as a judge by the conference and arrived last night.

Chen, Ye, and Others Arrive in Zhenjiang from Nanjing

Zhenjiang, 5th Telegram Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Ye Chuqiang, Shi Jingtang, and others arrived in Zhenjiang from Nanjing by private cars on the morning of the 5th to participate in the military inspection in the morning on the 6th. Salaries of Teachers in Secondary Schools Will Increase Next Semester

Abolish the Clock Hour System ... All Teachers Are Responsible for Moral Education

Nanjing, 5th Telegram The Ministry of Education has formulated a fourteen-article outline for the service and treatment methods of teachers and staff in secondary schools, and issued an order to the various departments and bureaus, which roughly stated that the administration of schools should strive for rationality and save the past waste on the salaries of teachers and staff, abolish the clock-hour pay system, increase the salaries of teachers, and the management of school affairs should be assigned to teachers to realize the spirit of joint school management by the Education Bureau and the principal. In terms of student moral education, we should strive to eliminate the past drawbacks of separating moral education from teaching, so that all teachers are responsible for moral education, and the principal should appoint a number of teachers to concurrently serve as moral education specialists to establish a foundation for personality education. However, China's territory is vast, and the situations in various places are different. The salary levels of teachers and staff in the middle schools of all provinces and cities, the assignment of school affairs to teachers, and the concurrent moral education matters should be reviewed and determined by the various departments and bureaus in accordance with local conditions as soon as possible in accordance with this outline. The Ministry will review and approve the single regulations, and the moral education methods of secondary schools across the country can be corrected from the next semester, and the salary methods for teachers will also be changed uniformly from the next school year, so that the efficiency of secondary education will be improved, and the entire education will also be promoted.

Provincial Party Department Fetes He Yingqin

Zhenjiang, 5th Telegram He Yingqin, Luo Jialun, and others came to the province in the afternoon of the 5th to participate in the grand military inspection on the morning of the 6th. The Provincial Party Department and the Provincial Government feted the members of the Central Committee who came to the province at the provincial office on the evening of the 5th.

Ministry of Education Orders All Regions to Quickly Form Sports Committees

Nanjing, 5th Telegram The Ministry of Education has announced the National Sports Implementation Plan. It is essential that the education departments and bureaus of provinces, cities, and counties listed in the plan should quickly establish sports committees. Therefore, the Ministry ordered all departments and bureaus to comply and ordered their subordinates to comply.

Li Yuying Will Arrive in London

To Attend the Opening Ceremony of the World Education Association

International Telegraph, 5th, Paris Telegram Li Yuying, representing the Chinese academic community, will accompany the Chinese Education Delegation to Europe from Geneva to London to attend the opening ceremony of the World Education Association and will consult with education experts from various countries attending the meeting on new world education.

Educational Inspection Team in Berlin

Havas Agency, Berlin, 4th Telegram The group of Cheng Qibao, Li Ximou, Yang Lian, Li Jiaxiang, and Guo Youshou, who were sent to Europe by the Chinese Ministry of Education to investigate education, arrived in Germany in early October and immediately went to Denmark, Poland, and major German cities such as Düsseldorf, Cologne, Stuttgart, Frankfurt, and Essen to visit primary and secondary schools, vocational schools, and other institutions for completing youth education. The education authorities provided courteous explanations and were tireless in seeking details. They have now completed the examination of the aforementioned places and are returning to Berlin to examine the administration of German universities and other schools, so that they can be used as a reference for China's education reform in the future. They will also examine the wireless telephone in Berlin. The survey team is very satisfied with this trip. According to Professor Cheng Qibao of Nanjing Central University, China is preparing to reform education, and this time, sending personnel to Europe to investigate is to use the results obtained as a reference for the future. However, China cannot completely adopt the European system, and in the future, it may take a compromise between the old and the new.
