The recent government news compilation of the Ministry of Education is as follows: 1) Ordered Feng Gangbai to go to various European countries to investigate art, and sent an official letter to the Chinese Embassy in the United Kingdom, etc., requesting instructions on everything. 2) Official letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting the embassies and consulates abroad to investigate the students studying in the countries and regions where they are stationed. 3) Official letter to the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan, sending the Ministry of Education's proposal to revise the draft organization law of the four types of primary and secondary schools, normal schools, and vocational schools into interim regulations, and the Executive Yuan will first announce the proposal. 4) Approved the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' reply, roughly stating that the request to exempt students from the three northeastern provinces from tuition for the current semester at the Wusong Merchant Marine School has been approved. 5) Executive Yuan's instructions, roughly stating that the Central Political Conference's letter on the resolution to add Wu Jingheng and others as members of the Northwest Specialized Education Construction Committee has been received and is hereby notified.

Local News

Private Schools in the French Concession Discuss Request for Subsidies

Establish a Joint Association of Primary and Secondary Private Schools in the Concession

Elected Executive and Supervisory Committee Members and Approved the Constitution

The Municipal Education Association Expresses Willingness to Cooperate

Private schools in the French Concession of this city held a joint meeting of private schools in the concession at the classroom of Huadong Middle School on Xujiahui Road yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, convened by Ma Jiazhen, the principal of Huadong Middle School, the initiator, to request subsidies from the French Municipal Council. More than 30 representatives from private schools attended. Ma Jiazhen was elected as the temporary chairman, and Ouyang Su was the recorder. After the etiquette was performed, the chairman first reported the purpose of convening the meeting, and then discussed the proposals and established the Joint Association of Private Primary and Secondary Schools in the French Concession, and elected the executive and supervisory committee members and approved the constitution on the spot. The details are recorded below:

Attending Representatives

The representatives of the attending private schools include: Middle schools: Ma Jiazhen (Huadong), Mao Zhaorong (Nanyang Advanced Commercial School), Zeng Kechen (Shanghai Women's Vocational School), Wu Yixin (Lehua), Hong Guang (Mingguang), Mao Jiaju (Tongyi), Ouyang Su (Zhiping), Ding Songcheng (Aesthetic), Gu Muzhou (Chenxi); Primary schools: Shen Junyang (Xinqun), Shen Xibin (Chongshi), Wu Jingbo (Xingzhong), Zhu Guowei (Zhonghe), Fu Tianmin (Simin Righteous School), Shi Chunyao (Zhicheng), Gong Ziyi (Tianhua), Du Shilu (Jianguo), Wang Zhen (Minsheng), Mao Yuanliang (Chenjing), Zheng Zhengde (Fuci), Liu Zhichao (Lisheng), Yang Di (Cotton Righteous Primary School), Shen Guang (Southeast), Shen Xiaofan (Zhejiang Shanghai), Xie Mengbo (Mengbo), Cheng Shijie (Guoben), Fei Pei (Qunhua), Mao Derun (Derun), Ye Zhiyi (Dunren), Wang Dingcheng (Dehua).

Important Resolutions

1) The case of the rapid organization and determination of the name of private schools in the concession. Resolution: Organize the Shanghai French Concession Private Primary and Secondary School Joint Association. 2) The case of electing representatives to draft the constitution on the spot. Resolution: Elect representatives from Nanyang Commercial School, Mingguang, and Tongyi to be responsible for drafting the constitution on the spot. 3) How to proceed with the request for subsidies from the French Municipal Council. Resolution: 1. Issue a declaration. 2. Invite newspaper reporters. 3. Request the Chinese directors and Chinese taxpayers' association to strive for it. 4. Submit a request to the Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Education Bureau, and the Municipal Education Association for assistance. 5. Regularly hold public banquets for Chinese directors and joint association dinners. 6. Send a letter to the French Consul General explaining the situation and requesting support. 4) The case of discussing and passing the drafted constitution of the association. Resolution: Amended and passed. 5) How to produce the executive and supervisory committee members of this association. Resolution: Elect double the number of people and vote by show of hands. As a result, Huadong, Nanyang Commercial School, Mingguang, Tongyi, Lehua, Xingzhong, Huiping, Chongshi, Chenxi, and other nine schools were elected as executive committee members. Dehua, Tianhua, Anshun, Dunren, Aesthetic, and other five schools were elected as supervisory committee members. 6) The case of drafting a declaration for the conference. Resolution: Handed over to the first joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees for handling. 7) The case of scheduling the first joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees. Resolution: Scheduled to be held at 7:00 PM on the 7th of this month (Monday), convened by Huadong.

Constitution Passed

Article 1: Name. The name of this association is the Shanghai French Concession Private Primary and Secondary School Joint Association. Article 2: Purpose. The purpose of this association is to connect feelings, promote education, and develop private schools. Article 3: Members. All private primary and secondary schools in the Shanghai French Concession may join this association as members. Article 4: Organization. Nine executive committee members are elected to form the executive committee. The executive committee members mutually elect three standing committee members to handle daily affairs. Five supervisory committee members are elected to form the supervisory committee. Article 5: Tasks. Detailed rules will be formulated separately. Article 6: Term of Office. Temporarily set for one year, with the possibility of re-election. Article 7: Session. A general meeting is held once per semester, at the beginning of the semester. However, in case of special matters, a meeting may be convened temporarily by the executive committee or at the request of three or more members. Article 8: Membership Fee. Each member shall pay a membership fee per semester, based on the number of grades. Middle schools: 2 yuan per grade; Primary schools: 1 yuan per grade. Article 9: Address. The address of this association is temporarily borrowed from the women's division of Huadong Middle School. Article 10: Supplementary Provisions. If there are any matters not covered in this constitution, they may be proposed by five or more members of the general meeting and amended with the consent of more than two-thirds of the members present.

Association Expresses

Yesterday, a reporter from the Shanghai News Agency specifically went to the Municipal Education Association to inquire about the association's opinion on this case. Huang Zaoxiong, the standing director of the association, received him and expressed his opinion, saying that it is true that private schools are restricted by funding and cannot develop school affairs. Chinese people in the French Concession pay a large amount of taxes every year, and the concession authorities should fulfill their obligation to cooperate with Chinese education. The subsidies obtained by private schools in the Public Concession are the result of the efforts of the Chinese directors. If the Chinese directors in the French Concession can also strive for Chinese education, they should have the same effect. The association stands on the ground of developing education and will naturally provide cooperation.

International Economic Statistics Society

Six Chinese Members

The International Economic Statistics Society is the central organization for international research on economic statistics. The president is Professor Fisher of the United States, and the vice president is Mr. Divisi of France. In terms of directors, there are economic statistics experts from Britain, Germany, Norway, and Poland. It is heard that those invited to join the association from China are He Lian from Tianjin, Liu Dajun and Cai Zhengya from Shanghai, and the China Review Weekly was entrusted to invite Sun Zheng, Zhang Xinyi, and Chen Huayin from Nanjing to join.

Pudong Middle School Teachers Recognize Monthly Donations to Aid Righteous Army

In view of the Northeast Volunteer Army's resistance against Japan and saving the country, Pudong Middle School, due to the lack of machinery, bullets, food, and grass, telegraphed for help. In the middle of last month, the teachers, staff, and students of the school raised more than 1,000 yuan and entrusted it to the Shanghai Bank for remittance to provide assistance. The matter has been reported in various newspapers. Now, teachers Wu Xianglong, Dai Yiqun, Chu Baohua, and others are discussing long-term fundraising methods to provide assistance. It was passed by the school affairs meeting on the 3rd of this month. Teachers and staff are free to recognize monthly donations, and for the students, the principal plans to submit it to the students for discussion during the next memorial week. There are more than 400 students in the school. The school plans to collect the funds at the end of the month and send them to the transferring agency.

A Grand Ceremony of Recognition at Shanghai Hujiang University

Education Bureau Director Pan Gives a Speech at the School

Shanghai Hujiang University held a recognition ceremony at the auditorium at 9:30 AM yesterday. Professors from each department and all students were in attendance. First, the patriotic song was sung, then President Liu described the significance of the ceremony, the purpose of which was to encourage students to work hard in their studies. Next, Shanghai Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan gave a speech, saying that selecting students with excellent grades at your esteemed university, listing their names on the honor roll, and holding a recognition ceremony is indeed a good way to encourage young people to work hard in their studies. He hoped that students would learn from and be grateful for the efforts of everyone, and use academic research as the foundation for future work. At the same time, he also hoped that students would pay attention to other aspects, take social life into consideration, gain rich experience, and learn the whole method of being a person, so as to transition through life, improve society, and correct the disease of being solely concerned with one's own moral perfection and the disintegration of public sentiment. This is the talent that China needs most today. College students should shoulder this responsibility, cultivate themselves well, and schools should especially train and reward talents who handle affairs for social groups. After he finished speaking, Dean Fan gave a report and presented certificates. Finally, the school song was sung and the meeting was adjourned. Among the students listed as honor students this year, girls accounted for 47 percent, and girls with the best grades accounted for 55 percent.

Shanghai School for Blind Children Celebrates 20th Anniversary

Also Holding Dedication Ceremony for New School Buildings

The Shanghai School for Blind Children, located at 290 Hongqiao Road in this city, was established in the second year of the Republic (1913). The original site was on Yidingpan Road. Since moving to Hongqiao Road, the school has extensively constructed new buildings. Yesterday, the school celebrated its 20th anniversary and held a dedication ceremony for the new buildings. At 4 PM, over 300 Chinese and foreign guests arrived successively. After refreshments, a meeting was held on the lawn of the schoolyard. First, Principal Fu Bulan, an American, and Director Fei Wusheng gave reports. Mayor Wu Tiecheng gave a speech, followed by performances by the blind children, including a four-part chorus, violin solo, group exercises, and human pyramids. Finally, the school song was sung and the meeting was adjourned. The school displayed various rattan wares made by the blind children, with elegant styles and low prices, which were praised and enthusiastically purchased by the guests.

Navy's Strength Suddenly Increases; Donghua Barely Wins

Result: 3 to 0

No Achievements in the First Half

In the Western League Football Association, the strength of the British Navy is unpredictable. Those who were mediocre and incompetent yesterday may transform into a strong and powerful team today. This is because the troops are transferred from time to time, and the strength of the team also changes from time to time. This has been clearly proven in previous years. Even the Navy this year was incompetent, having lost to Jinan 0-11. However, the Navy that played against Donghua at the baseball field yesterday was a strong and powerful team. It was a combined team of Conto and Kaituo, who had recently come to Shanghai. The Conto fleet defeated the Lehua in its heyday with a score of 2-1. Although its strength has slightly decreased, it is still a strong team. Therefore, neither side scored in the first half of yesterday's match. In the second half, Donghua spared no effort to score three consecutive goals and win the final victory. Generally, football fans thought that yesterday's match would be uninteresting, and only a few thousand people came to the scene. However, those who witnessed the battle were all amazed. Here is a record of the fierce battle:

Chen Hongguang Misses Three Times

With the sound of the horn, the three armies

lined up. Donghua was in the south, with the wind helping, and launched a major attack on the north. Li Yichen broke through the encirclement, with Chen Wanliang on both sides. Henry could not stop them and asked Du Foyer for help, and the ball was cleared out of danger. Feng Yunyou was loyal and courageous, and his passing was appropriate. Wan Xianghua crossed the ball, and Chen Hongguang used his head to attack, but unfortunately it went over the crossbar and became a wild ball. Long Lei did not kick the ball far, and Wu Youliang intercepted it midway and passed it to Yu Tian. Henry and two enemy generals rushed out of the kickoff line, and the inside was empty. Yichen and Xiaowan marched quickly to the shooting area and threw the ball to Hongguang, who headed the ball again, but it became a wild ball. In less than two minutes, Chen Hongguang rushed into the enemy's territory alone. Feng Yunyou got the ball and shot at the gate from afar. Hongguang caught up and accelerated, but the ball passed by the gate three times without entering.

Li Yiju First Captures Enemy City

The British army struggled in the stormy waves

for more than ten minutes and was fortunate not to fall into the trap. They then launched a major counterattack and attacked our position several times. Li Ning worked hard, and Guan Xun'an did not give way, preventing the enemy from entering our territory. After the break, the British army took advantage of the favorable wind and their attack became brave and sharp, often entering our area. However, because the forward did not have agile feet, they repeatedly failed to succeed. After a fierce battle for fifteen minutes, Tu Kaiyuan shouted and mobilized the troops, and Feng Yunyou provided support from behind. Chen Jiaqiu dribbled the ball past Henry and passed it far to Xiaowan. Du Foyer stepped forward, but the ball had already been crossed. Li Yichen headed the ball into the goal on the Long Lei line, and the score was opened.

Wan Xianghua Makes Another Miraculous Contribution

Although the enemy lost a city,

their momentum became more arrogant. Qu Lu and Ge Liying were especially brave, attacking the iron gate five or six times, but all failed. Before long, Li Ning kicked a ball out of the inner guard line, and Tu Kaiyuan quickly passed it to Hongguang. After three passes, the ball was obtained by Wan Xianghua, who was as fast as a galloping horse. Taifo tried his best to entangle him but could not. Sankai also lost ground one after another. Xiaowan entered the no-man's land and hurriedly raised his foot to knock on the door. Long Lei could not stop him, and the ball entered the goal from the upper left corner, clear and sharp, which was very wonderful.

Fulan Mu Misunderstands and Misses an Opportunity

After Donghua scored two goals,

they were radiant and handy, and invincible. Although Henry was brave, he was old and weak. He could still cope with the first half without any errors, but in the second half, he was embarrassed. In addition, with two cities lost, the soldiers had no will to fight, and the inner guard line was especially chaotic. Before long, Chen Yutian went deep alone and passed the ball to Jiaqiu at a suitable spot. For some reason, Fulan Mu was stunned and did not save the ball. Li Yichen scored another goal. The ball bounced off Fulan Mu's back and entered the goal. The goalkeeper fell to the ground to save it, but it was too late. Before the battle was over, the war clouds were gloomy and the sound of the horn rose. Donghua sang another triumphant song.

Wu Ben Defeats Haixing Again in Charity Volleyball Tournament

|Result: 3 to 1|

Qinglian Also Defeats Czech 3 to 1

Yesterday's charity volleyball matches for men and women began at 1:30 PM at the China Basketball Hall. As a result, Wu Ben defeated Haixing again with a score of 3-1, and Qinglian also defeated Czech with a score of 3-1. Here is a summary of the situation:

Women's Group

First Set

Starting at 1:30 PM, the women took to the court first. Haixing took the initiative and took the lead, taking the advantage with 11-10 in the first half of the set. After changing direction, the competition between the two sides became more intense, with blocks and kills, and wonderful moments. Later, the score became a 14-14 tie. Haixing once again took the lead with 16-15, but eventually lost to Wu Ben with a score of 19-21.

Second Set

Haixing had a solid lineup and good delivery, with Haixing scoring 11 points in the first half of the set, while Wu Ben only scored 5 points. As a result, Haixing won the set with a score of 21-9, quite easily.

Third Set

The competition in this set was even more intense. However, Haixing was mostly in the lead in the first half of the set, but failed in the second half. Among them, Haixing had a chance to win with a score of 16-11, but lost the opportunity due to excessive haste. Wu Ben still caught up and reversed the defeat with a score of 21-18.

Fourth Set

Wu Ben took the lead with 6-1, but was caught up by Haixing, tying the score at 10-10. Wu Ben won the first half of the set and continued to lead from then on, quite smoothly. As a result, they won again with a score of 21-15.

Middle School Tennis Championship: Fudan Shizhong Wins

Defeats Hujiang 2-0

The 4th Shanghai Middle School Tennis League has been underway for several days since the start of the championship. The winners of the final were Hujiang Affiliated Middle School and Fudan Shizhong. The two schools held the final at the China Tennis Court at 3 PM yesterday. Both sides had young players and new talents, so the battle was quite exciting. After a fierce battle of more than an hour, Fudan Shizhong won both singles matches and defeated Hujiang 2-0, winning the championship. Hujiang, which had held the championship for three years, was shaken today, and the brilliant championship trophy was moved from Yangshupu to Jiangwan Road, which is a new change in the history of middle school tennis. After the match, Ms. Zhao Shaonan was invited to present the awards. Here are the results of the two singles matches and the overall match results:

(1) Liang Deguang (Fudan Shizhong) 6-1, 6-0 Wu Guoxiang (Hujiang)

(2) Ma Canzhou (Fudan Shizhong) 6-0, 6-0 Tang Zhihuai (Hujiang)

Fudan Shizhong Championship Team (Photo by Chen Bingde)

(From right to left) Lin Zhaoguang (Secretary), Situ Qiu, Chen Chao, Ma Candan, Liang Deguang, Tang Hu.

Five Years of Memories

In terms of the team... Hujiang is the best

Talking about individuals... talents emerge in large numbers

The Shanghai Middle School Sports Association was established in the winter of the 16th year of the Republic of China (1927) and has a history of five years. It has held four tennis leagues, and with the advocacy and encouragement of various schools, it has cultivated many young tennis talents, who are active in the tennis world. For example, Yu Tianguang and He Shengting were small heroes who won the championship for Hujiang in those years. Over the years, Mr. Yu has leapt to become one of the top figures in Shanghai. In addition, Qian Yaobin of Guanghua once fought to the death with Yu Tianguang many times in middle school. Mr. Qian's skills are also one of the best in Shanghai today. Others, such as Deng You of Guanghua and Xie Quanhe of Jinan, all came from here and are now the main players in the university tennis competition. Since the opening of this year's league, another comet has been discovered, namely Liang Deguang of Fudan Shizhong, who is young and highly skilled and is appreciated by general connoisseurs. Even the veteran Wang Qulin has praised him as a rising star with great potential. In terms of the team, Hujiang has won the championship for three consecutive years. In terms of individuals, talents have emerged from all sides. At the end of the tennis competition, I have written this in a haphazard manner to commemorate the event. (Qian)

All Countries Are Secretly Striving for the International Race Walking

To Be Held on December 4th

Municipal Government Telegraphs the Executive Yuan to Stop Extending Loans for American Wheat

Grain Prices Plunge, Efforts Underway to Provide Relief

Dumping of American Wheat Severely Damages the Economy

The Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday telegraphed the Executive Yuan on behalf of the Nanjing Executive Yuan: "Respectfully, according to a report from the Bureau of Social Affairs, concerning a petition. Based on a report from the Grain Committee, also concerning a petition. At the 37th regular meeting of the Committee, a temporary motion was made regarding the disastrous fall in grain prices, requesting that the Central Government refrain from further borrowing American wheat to avoid harming the agricultural economy. The motion resolved to present a report requesting a halt to the reported plan of the Central Government to borrow American wheat, etc. An investigation reveals that, according to various newspapers, the matter involves discussions between a US advisor to the Ministry of Finance and the Shanghai representative of the US Finance Corporation for Rehabilitation regarding the amount of the extended loan and the methods of transportation to China. The total amount of the extended loan is approximately 450,000 tons, valued at US$12 million, equivalent to CN¥50 million. If this is true, the impact on the domestic rural economy will be significant. Moreover, this year's harvest in various regions is relatively abundant, and grain prices have plummeted. The Central Government is striving to implement relief measures. If a large amount of American wheat is transported to China for sale, domestic grain prices will inevitably fall further, reaching a point beyond recovery. The rural economy will be on the verge of irreversible destruction, and the farmers, who account for 80% of the national population, will face bankruptcy. The Committee feels deeply concerned and cannot remain silent. Therefore, we respectfully submit the resolved motion to Your Excellency, requesting your prompt review and a telegraph to the Central Government to halt the proposed extension of the American wheat loan, etc. Accordingly, an investigation of the minutes of the 37th meeting of the Committee shows that the report has already been submitted for review and filing. Based on the report, in addition to instructions, we respectfully submit a report for your review, which is deemed to be in the public interest, etc. Accordingly, an investigation reveals that this year's harvest in various regions is relatively abundant, and grain prices have plummeted. Efforts are currently underway to provide relief, which is already a challenge. If, as reported, American wheat is further loaned, transported to China, and dumped, domestic grain prices will inevitably fall further, significantly impacting the domestic agricultural economy. Therefore, careful consideration is essential. Based on the report, in addition to instructions, we respectfully submit a telegraph for your review and guidance. Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai, bowing, seal."

Li Du Telegraphs War Situation

Self-Defense Army Occupies Fujin

Liu Piguang, the Shanghai representative of General Li Du, received a telegram yesterday from Li regarding the war situation at the front. The translated original telegram recorded by the Riri (Daily News) is as follows: (Omitted above) 1. Li Xiaotong, the commander-in-chief of the Yilan region, led the Lu Yongcai and Chen Zongdai brigades to inflict a major defeat on the enemy forces at the Battle of Tulong Mountain. The small detachment stationed in Fujin showed signs of activity, fearing that our troops would pursue and advance on Jiamusi and Yilan, etc., to create a remote diversion. The Wang Ruishu regiment of our Lu Yongcai brigade, on October 21st, circled behind the enemy forces in Fujin, launching a fierce surprise attack. The enemy forces responded with full force, engaging in fierce combat for four days and nights. The enemy forces were unable to withstand the attack and retreated along the river. On the dawn of October 26th, Fujin was occupied by our troops. In this battle, 38 enemy soldiers were killed, and an uncalculated number were wounded. We also captured one heavy machine gun and several dozen rifles. Our side also suffered casualties. After a brief period of reorganization, we plan to join forces with our troops currently moving along the river to advance on Jiamusi, Yilan, etc. 2. The Songhua River area has been severely disturbed by enemy and puppet troops. Compounding this, the recent floods have made life unbearable for our people. The Japanese army has recently used large sums of money to bribe puppet officials and unscrupulous merchants to purchase large quantities of grain at high prices from various locations along the river, transporting it to Harbin and then transferring it elsewhere. After suffering from war and disaster, agricultural production in various areas along the river is only one or two out of ten. Farmers, due to livelihood concerns, have no choice but to sell as much as possible. Under these circumstances, even without war or natural disasters next year, the seeds for the people will become a problem. Our troops face increasing difficulties. This policy of the Japanese army can be described as extremely vicious. 3. From the beginning of the invasion of Northeast China, the Japanese army has actively implemented armed immigration, but immigration is only a name, and the reality is the concealment of troops. According to our recent investigations, Japanese immigrants in the Jiamusi area are freely occupying our people's land or expelling our good people from the country under the pretext of reactionary or other crimes, and then transferring their land to Japanese immigrants. After obtaining large amounts of land, these Japanese immigrants either hire Korean laborers to cultivate the land or force our people to work. They are completely engaged in military affairs. This situation is clearly a disguised form of troop increase and armed robbery, but they call it immigration, which is too much of a self-deception. (Omitted below)

Li Du and Ding Chao's Representative, Su Chun, Makes a Statement

Li's Directly Controlled National Defense Army Totals 50,000 Men

Tenaciously Defending Twelve Counties, Fighting a Desperate Battle Against the Enemy

Generals Li Du and Ding Chao recently sent a representative, Su Chun, south to report to the Central Government on the anti-Japanese situation of the Jilin Self-Defense Army. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday from Beijing and immediately reported to various circles in the city and various mass organizations to express gratitude for their assistance and to discuss all matters. The Riri (Daily News) reporter met with Mr. Su yesterday, and he provided a detailed account of the situation in Jilin. The following is a record: The Northeast Incident has passed for over a year. In Jilin, Generals Li and Ding rose up to resist the Japanese, and the righteous armies responded. The Japanese invaders were exhausted from running around. They only guarded the railway lines and important cities, relying on their sophisticated equipment and powerful firepower to simultaneously attack and defend, waiting for us to be trapped and put to death. If we do not receive sufficient assistance, it will be difficult to maintain a long-term and unwearying resistance against the enemy. On behalf of Generals Li and Ding, I disguised myself and came south to report the recent situation of the Jilin army to all circles in Shanghai, representing all the soldiers and expressing our sincere gratitude for the enthusiasm of the Shanghai circles in their past assistance. We also request continued supplies to strengthen our forces, so that we can fight a desperate battle against the bandits. Deputy Commander Li is currently stationed in Muleng Lishuzhen, commanding military operations at the front. Chairman Ding is stationed in Boli, touring various counties and managing the entire administration. As for all the troops within the scope of the Self-Defense Army, excluding the units led by Feng Zhanhai and others who are operating as guerrillas in various locations, Li's directly controlled units consist of nine fully equipped mixed brigades of the National Defense Army, totaling approximately 50,000 men, distributed in various locations at the front. In addition, 20 security regiments, totaling approximately 30,000 men, are organized in various counties in the rear. They are all equipped with weapons, but ammunition is lacking. In the twelve counties defended by Ding and Li, the area is over 3,000 li in circumference. Within this area, the Blue Sky with a White Sun national flag is displayed everywhere, the people continue to work as usual, schools are still open, and postal communications are unimpeded. Li has also specially dispatched a cavalry regiment to patrol and suppress bandits, so the local security is very good. Chickens and dogs are not alarmed. This is truly the only intact area in the Northeast. However, due to the inconvenience of foreign trade, there is a great lack of materials. Li has a strong force, and his subordinates are strictly disciplined. Cooperation between officials and the people is very harmonious. If the government and the compatriots throughout the country can provide them with sufficient assistance, they will be able to resist the enemy for a long time. The weather in the Northeast is quite cold, and it is now covered with ice and snow. If the Songhua River freezes solid, the Japanese fleet will become ineffective, and we will be able to break through the enemy in Yilan. At the same time, we have a liaison plan with Chairman Ma and Commander Su. When the two sides meet, Jilin and Heilongjiang can be united into one, and the recovery of northern Manchuria is truly a matter of time. Currently, Li Xiaotong, the deputy chief of staff of the headquarters, is serving as the commander-in-chief of the Yilan area and has crossed Fujin and Huachuan, approaching Yilan. The enemy and insurgents in Yilan will soon be wiped out. In the past, the Japanese army built a very strong motor road from Dunhua to Ning'an, originally intending to use this road to utilize tanks and armored vehicles, but it has now been seized by the forces of Ma Xianzhang, the commander-in-chief of the road, and Liu Wankui, the deputy commander. The Japanese troops stationed in various locations in Jilin only dare to operate along the railway and dare not leave the vicinity. Currently, with the exception of a few cities that are fiercely occupied by the Japanese army, the remaining towns and cities are all within the sphere of influence of the Self-Defense Army. Even the few bandits scattered in various counties in western Jilin have anti-Japanese hearts and cooperate with the government troops. That bandits can do this is also very admirable. As for the Big Sword Society, they are all organized by the brave people, and the tens of thousands of troops trained by Xing Zhanqing and Yang Yaojun are especially elite. Li plans to expand the organization and training, so that every citizen of Jilin will be a staunch anti-Japanese element, so as to resist the Japanese for a long time without fatigue. Currently, there is a small-scale ordnance factory in the rear of our army, manufacturing landmines, hand grenades, bombs, etc. As for the bullets used for rifles, because there is no copper shell machine, we can only collect discarded bullet shells and carry out the procedure of loading medicine by hand, so the results are not as good as the manufacture of hand grenades, etc. Wherever I passed, the soldiers were stationed in trenches or underground tunnels, suffering greatly, but without complaint. These are soldiers fighting for the survival of the nation, which is truly admirable and fills me with infinite emotion. I previously went to various places in the Northeast to investigate and felt that within the scope of Li and Ding, military and government affairs were in order, and the people did not feel pain, so they also joined the work. I was quite moved by the sincerity of Generals Li and Ding towards their subordinates, and the subordinates all obeyed orders and did their duty. Therefore, the Japanese army's forces have not been able to reach the twelve counties in eastern Jilin. On September 20th, I was ordered to enter the pass to report, but because I walked over 1,600 li, the arrival was relatively late. I have previously held military and political positions in various places in Jiangsu and Anhui. This year, in February, I was indignant at the Japanese pirates' endless aggression and had a responsibility to save the country, so I asked for leave to go out of the pass and join the Self-Defense Army, hoping to do my best.

Temporary Martial Law Tomorrow

November 7th is the 15th anniversary of the establishment of the Soviet government in Russia. Wen Hongsi, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, received reports beforehand that the Communist Party in the city would take action. In order to strictly prevent this, he ordered the police stations in each district, the police brigade, and the detective units to strengthen precautions in advance. At that time, all units would be dispatched, and temporary martial law would be declared. He also discussed joint defense measures with the police departments of the Public Concession and the French Concession. At that time, temporary martial law would be declared throughout the city, and meetings and parades would be prohibited.

Over 100 Public Associations in the City Request Punishment of Customs Officials

Over one hundred trade associations in the city believe that the Jianghai Customs has exceeded its authority and harassed businesses. They previously sent representatives to Beijing to petition, which was reported in various newspapers. It has now been heard that the various trade associations believe that Robert Ford, the Customs Commissioner, and George Wright, the Deputy Customs Commissioner, of the Maritime Customs, have used their own personal intentions to exceed their authority and harass businesses. Tang Haian, the Superintendent of Huai Customs, has sat idly by while businesses were harassed and has failed to correct the situation, neglecting his duties. At a meeting of the chairmen of the various trade associations a few days ago, it was resolved to jointly file a complaint with the National Government's Executive Yuan, Control Yuan, and Ministry of Finance, requesting that Customs Commissioner Robert Ford, Deputy Customs Commissioner George Wright, and Customs Superintendent Tang Haian be dismissed from their posts and handed over for disciplinary action to appease public anger. The original petition states: "We, the undersigned, petition concerning the matter of Jianghai Customs searching for smuggled goods and tax evasion, which has recently exceeded its scope and intruded into shops, causing widespread harassment. Representatives from various industries have been jointly dispatched to the relevant departments in the capital to petition on this matter. Although there are no complete tariff laws and regulations to study the scope of the Customs' authority to search for tax evasion, a rough outline can be obtained by examining various sources. For the purpose of suppressing smuggling, the Customs has specially established several patrol boats for the use of Customs police. This demonstrates that the execution of duties is limited to the Customs ports under its jurisdiction. This is sufficient proof. Among the national agencies that handle tax collection and are similar to the Customs, there were formerly Likin stations and regular customs, and now there are Unified Tax Bureaus in various districts. Likin stations and regular customs only inspected ships or merchants, not shops. Unified Tax Bureaus only inspect goods leaving factories and not retailers. This is because their powers are limited. Even with regard to the Customs itself, it has been seventy or eighty years since customs were established for trade. Could it be that the commissioners who served in the past completely disregarded tax collection, or that the importers of the past were completely unable to engage in profiteering? However, for seventy or eighty years, there has never been a case of searching shops, because the customs officials at that time were still able to adhere to the limits of authority granted to them by laws and regulations, and they were still able to fulfill their duties of searching goods upon entry into the port, rarely engaging in favoritism. Therefore, there was no need to exceed the scope and disturb shops. Therefore, if the Customs claims that there has been a recent increase in tax evasion, it can only blame the dereliction of duty of its subordinates and urgently think of ways to rectify the situation. It cannot use this as an excuse to exceed the scope. Goods entering the hands of shops have already separated from the importer and entered the retail merchant, and under current law, they only have the obligation to pay business tax. The authority to inspect them already belongs to the Business Tax Bureau. Recently, Sir Frederick Maze, the Inspector General of Customs, in view of the criticisms of public opinion, has misrepresented that searching shops is also practiced in various countries in the East and West, and is not an innovation of Jianghai Customs. These few words are sufficient to prove that the search of shops by Jianghai Customs not only lacks a legal basis, but also has not obtained the permission of the competent department. Therefore, he misrepresents the practice in various countries in the East and West in order to conceal his shortcomings. The power of officials is granted by the state and cannot be created by the officials themselves. If it is considered that this precedent should be adopted, it can only contribute opinions for the competent department to adopt. It cannot be implemented arbitrarily based on one's own personal intentions. The Customs is an agency that implements laws and regulations, not an agency that creates laws and regulations. Based on the above arguments, Customs Commissioner Robert Ford and Deputy Customs Commissioner George Wright of Jianghai Customs have acted illegally and exceeded their authority in handling this matter, and according to administrative regulations, there is reason for them to be subject to disciplinary action. As for the handling of tax collection matters in various trading ports, according to Article 7 of the Regulations for Employing Foreigners to Assist in Customs Affairs in the Third Year of Tongzhi, it is stated that "All public affairs should be managed by the Superintendent." However, the Customs Superintendent has sat idly by while they acted illegally and exceeded their authority. Although merchants have repeatedly appealed, he has not said a word of correction, which is also a neglect of duty. Therefore, we jointly request that your Yuan and Departments deliver them for disciplinary action to warn those in positions of authority, which is truly in the public interest. Respectfully submitted to the Executive Yuan, Control Yuan, and Ministry of Finance by the Shanghai Silk Gloss Cotton Weaving Industry, Chinese Soap Industry, Silk Industry, Department Store Industry, Foreign Firm Tea Industry, Silk Printing Industry, Printing and Canning Industry, Thermos Bottle Manufacturing Industry, Textile Machinery Industry, Woolen Factory Industry, Tobacco Exchange Industry, Coal Industry, Knitting Industry, Eyeglasses Industry, Watch Industry, Bamboo Industry, Travel Industry, Tea and Food Industry, Sand and Stone Industry, Electrical Appliance Industry, Lumber Industry, Biscuit and Candy Industry, Local Goods Industry, Freight Car Industry, Transfer Industry, New Medicine Industry, Fruit Industry, Retail Grain Industry, Chicken and Duck Industry, Rice Store Industry, Ginseng and Bird's Nest Industry, Dry Tobacco Industry, Fresh Pork Industry, Sugar Industry, Pen and Ink Industry, Straw Hat Industry, Pollen Industry, Construction Factory Industry, Homespun Industry, Local Yellow Wine Industry, Garment Industry, Blacksmith Industry, Silk Thread Industry, Jewelry Industry, Fresh Music Industry, Shoe Industry, Longan Industry, Tobacco Leaf Industry, Cotton Cloth Industry, Mineral Ash Industry, North-South Goods Industry, Flour Mill Industry, Candle Industry, Yarn and Sock Dyeing Industry, Woolen Industry, Paper Industry, Sausage Industry, Flying Flower Industry, and over one hundred and fifty other trade associations."

Customs Building Ships to Suppress Smuggling

Due to Rampant Smuggling and Tax Evasion

The North-China Daily News states that the tax rate on ordinary commodities under the old tariff regulations was very low, so the number of smugglers of ordinary commodities was limited. After the implementation of the new tariff regulations, smugglers of goods that did not pay taxes could obtain huge profits, and well-organized smuggling organizations were established one after another. Smuggled goods were no longer limited to jade, opium, morphine, military equipment, and valuable luxury goods. Even ordinary daily necessities could obtain huge profits through smuggling. Smuggling organizations charge fees according to the value of the goods, and many people are happy to use them, so their income is also very abundant. In the past two years, these people have been extremely active, and the number of ordinary commodities they smuggle is extremely large, but it is currently impossible to estimate the exact number. Recently, the shops searched by the Shanghai Customs have mostly been jewelry stores and watch stores. These items are easy to hide and are often placed in passengers' luggage or hidden on their persons. Some are also hidden in bulky goods, with ingenious designs that are not easy to detect. Mail parcels are also convenient for smuggling small items. Hong Kong and Dalian are now free ports and are close to various ports in China, so smugglers have used these places to establish headquarters. Today, most of the smuggling organizations in China are operated by Chinese, but some foreigners are also engaged in this business. According to news from the Hong Kong correspondent of the North-China Daily News, smuggling between Guangzhou and Hong Kong has been extremely rampant recently, and some even use political figures as protectors. Other ports along the South China coast are also connected to Hong Kong for smuggling, and the number is very large. The Customs is currently stepping up its prevention of this type of smuggling. Although it cannot be said to be as complete as the prevention system in Europe and America, it has already achieved remarkable results. The Customs has specially built many patrol boats for this purpose, some of which have been completed and put into use, and some are still under construction. On June 8th of this year, Mrs. Maze held a launching ceremony for a new patrol boat. Its interior has long been completely installed, and it was test-driven outside Wusongkou at the beginning of last month, and its speed is quite fast. There is also a sister ship of the same type, which is being built at the Jiangnan Shipyard and is about to be completed. It is expected that it will also be able to test-drive and be received this month. The customs officers on the new patrol boats have received strict training in the use of firearms, etc., to increase their effectiveness. According to a recent report from a new patrol boat inspecting the northern seas, the smuggling of sugar in Tianjin, Yantai, and other ports has been curbed due to strict inspections, and the price of sugar sold on the market has returned to normal prices and is no longer as low as the wholesale price as it was a few months ago. Now that the customs authorities have added patrol boats and stepped up prevention, it is expected that the trend of smuggling can be gradually suppressed and tax revenue can also be increased. At present, the tax expenses of European countries often increase sharply due to anti-smuggling measures. For example, Germany spends 30% of its total tax revenue on anti-smuggling expenses. The percentage of China's Customs' anti-smuggling expenses cannot be determined at present, but it is probably less than one-tenth of that of Germany.

Mrs. Li Jishen and Others Initiate the Women's Relief Northeast Association

Mr. Li Jishen, who has consistently advocated resistance against Japan, could not bear to sit idly by after hearing of the tragic situation in the Northeast. His wife, Li Zhou Yueqing, possessed with compassion, especially invited Mrs. Song Zhen, the wife of the former Guangdong Governor Zhang Woquan, and widely invited the wives of various important figures to organize the Women's Relief Northeast Association. Those who signed up to join the initiators included Mrs. Chen Shuying, the wife of Sun Ke, Mrs. Chen Zhu Guangzhen, the wife of Chen Mingshu, and Mrs. Huang Yuru, the wife of Dai Ji, etc. Wu Mai, who kowtowed to the 19th Route Army, showed his respect to Mrs. Li and specially hosted a banquet at No. 42, Jiaozhou Road, to express his appreciation. Mr. Li Liejun, Zhang Zhiben, Xue Dubi, Shi Liangcai, and others who were present praised her without exception. Mrs. Li plans to visit the wives of leaders from all walks of life with Ms. Song and ask them to mobilize together, so that at least over a million can be raised to see in practical terms in the near future. Such a heroic woman can make the men feel ashamed. The full text of its simple charter is recorded below: Charter of the Chinese Women's Relief Northeast Association: (Article 1) Name: This association is named the Chinese Women's Relief Northeast Association. (Article 2) Purpose: The purpose of this association is to unite Chinese women to relieve Northeast compatriots. (Article 3) Membership: Those who agree with the purpose of this association can be introduced by a member to become a member. (Article 4) Organization: This association uses a committee system, with five to seven members, including one to three standing committee members. First, a number of honorary committee members are appointed. The standing committee is divided into the following groups: 1. General Affairs Group, 2. Publicity Group, 3. Fundraising Group, 4. Relief Group. The detailed rules for each group will be formulated separately. (Article 5) Membership Fees: Each member pays a one-time membership fee of one yuan and an annual regular fee of one yuan. Donations and special donations are not subject to this rule. The office expenses of this association are generally borne by colleagues, and no donation money will be used. (Article 6) Meeting Dates: Regular meetings are held once a month, and general meetings are held once a year. Special meetings are held when necessary. All meetings are convened by the Standing Committee. (Article 7) Meeting Place: The headquarters is located at No. 16 Aivenfang, Aivenyi Road, Shanghai. Branches are established in various places when necessary. (Article 8) Report: All donations received by this association are first paid to the temporary receipt by the handler, and the official receipt of this association is exchanged as proof. A report is made once a month at the regular meeting. At the end of the year, in addition to publishing in the newspaper, a letter of credit will be printed and published separately. (Article 9) This charter will be implemented after being passed by the founding assembly. (Article 10) If there are any matters not covered in this charter, the Standing Committee will propose revisions.

Internally, blood and ammunition are insufficient, and externally, relief is lacking. The situation is extremely difficult. Our association is using our meager strength to respond to the Righteous Army's call for support from home and abroad. In the past six months, although we have successively provided relief to the Righteous Army in Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang with the proceeds from donations, totaling approximately 200,000 yuan, the amount is not much and still feels like a drop in the bucket. Guangdong and Guangxi are the source of the revolution, and the unwavering anti-Japanese and national salvation sentiments are a model for the whole country. Mayor Wu Held a Banquet Last Night for Various Sectors to Discuss Relief for the Three Provinces Disaster Area

Nine people, including Wen Lanting, were elected

to establish a Preparatory Office for the Disaster Area Inspection Group

The three provinces of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei have suffered from communist bandit disasters for several years. At the beginning of June this year, the central government, adhering to the principle of pacifying the interior before resisting foreign aggression, ordered a general suppression. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek also went to Hubei Province to supervise the campaign, and military victories were achieved one after another, with the disaster areas gradually being recovered. However, the people were displaced, and the fields and homes were in ruins. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, recognizing that the disaster had already occurred and that famine was a cause for concern, telegraphed Wang Xiaolai, a leader of the Shanghai business community, to Xunyang to discuss the matter, resulting in the organization of the Shanghai Temporary Relief Association for the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Disaster Areas. Mayor Wu, Zhang Gongquan, and leaders from various sectors were invited to serve as members of the association. In order to plan all the implementation measures, Mayor Wu and others hosted a banquet at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce at 7:00 PM yesterday, inviting over a hundred representatives from various sectors and organizations. During the banquet, representatives from the three provinces of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei reported on the disaster situation in their respective provinces, and nine people, including Wen Lanting and Liu Zhanen, were elected to establish a Preparatory Office for the Three Provinces Disaster Area Inspection Group, so that people from all walks of life could join in to inspect the real situation. The details are listed below:

Relief Declaration

A declaration from the Shanghai Temporary Relief Association for the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Disaster Areas reads: Alas, our people have suffered from banditry for a long time. South of the Yellow River and north of the Yangtze River, cities and towns have been reduced to ruins, ancestral graves have been destroyed, the old and weak have been slaughtered, women have been driven away and humiliated, property has been completely plundered, livelihoods have been gradually cut off, and people and animals have been completely wiped out. Woe is me! Who did this? Who caused this? To make the tens of thousands of poor people in our several-thousand-mile disaster areas in three provinces displaced, destitute, and suffering to such an extreme? The ferocity of the disaster is so severe that, looking back to ancient times and surveying the world, there has never been a disaster as widespread and cruel as the current situation in the disaster-stricken areas of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei. Recently, Chief Military Commissioner Chiang, with his resolute spirit, has been engaged in the work of suppression for several months, and has gradually recovered Shangcheng, Guangshan, and Gushi in Henan, Yingshan, Huoqiu, Liu'an, and Huoshan in Anhui, and Huang'an, Macheng, Luotian, Mianyang, and Jianli in Hubei, which can also be said to have been difficult. However, with thousands of miles of devastation and millions of displaced people, who will pacify them? Who will comfort them? Although this is the responsibility of the authorities, it is also something that benevolent gentlemen cannot bear to sit idly by. Telegrams are sent from all directions, and reports come from all sides. Saving lives and alleviating suffering is a duty that cannot be shirked. This is why we have organized the Temporary Relief Association for the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Disaster Areas. Everyone wants to do good. Who is not like us? To pull people out of fire and water and put them on a bed of comfort, who can we rely on if not our fathers, elders, siblings, aunts, and sisters at home and abroad? This declaration is respectfully submitted for your consideration.

Mayor Wu's Report

Mayor Wu, representing the Temporary Relief Association for the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Disaster Areas, gave the first report, saying: Today, our association is hosting this banquet for all representatives to seek relief for the disaster victims in the three provinces. Since the September 18th Incident in Shenyang last year, the public has been stirred up and focused on diplomatic issues, while neglecting internal problems, resulting in a failure to concentrate our strength to cope with this unprecedentedly serious situation. This situation is a combination of foreign troubles (i.e., the Northeast problem) and internal worries (i.e., the communist bandit problem). The people in the disaster areas of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei were either incited by poor politics or seduced by the communist bandits' propaganda (robbing the rich to help the poor) a few years ago, not realizing that they were opening the door to thieves. However, wherever the communist bandits went, they concentrated cash and food, forcing many people to flee to avoid starvation. As a result, the communist bandits' power expanded. This summer's general suppression has confined the communist bandits to a corner, so they are now engaged in looting. Therefore, the recovered areas are now a scorched earth. The fundamental task of restoring the disaster areas and eliminating the power of the communist bandits is to appease the displaced people and prevent the civilians who have been deceived by the communist bandits from being misled by their propaganda again. The significance of this relief is even greater. I hope that everyone will be generous and donate generously.

Reports on the Disaster Situations

After Mayor Wu's report, he

invited Sun Chunzhai and other representatives to report on the disaster situation in the three provinces. Sun Chunzhai said that the disaster-stricken areas in Anhui Province include Liu'an, Huoqiu, Huoshan, and Yingshan counties. The tragic situation there is beyond our imagination. Recently, there has been the organization of the "Bare Egg Society" in various places, which gathers villagers in one village to rob food from neighboring villages. When the food is exhausted, the villagers of that village go to other villages to rob food. After several such rounds, they can gather tens of thousands of people. The suffering can be imagined. Li Zizhong reported that the disaster-stricken areas in Henan Province include Shangcheng, Guangshan, Gushi, Luoshan, Xinyang, Xixian, and Huangchuan, with Huangchuan and Shangcheng being the most severely affected. When the communist bandits were entrenched, they concentrated property and forced the people to flee for food. Now that the communist bandits have been suppressed and are fleeing, although Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has ordered the pacification, the people's property has been plundered, and the fields and homes are in ruins. Even if they return, they have no clothes or food and cannot cultivate the land. Therefore, many go to Hankou to beg. Liu Zhanen reported on the disaster situation in Hubei Province, saying that although only Huang'an, Macheng, Luotian, Mianyang, and Jianli are considered disaster-stricken areas in Hubei Province, the impact on areas outside these five is also very significant. The tragedy is even worse than that of the Songhu area after the January 28th Incident, but because of the distance, the true situation is not clear. I hope that the gentry and scholars in Shanghai will not stand idly by, thinking that it has nothing to do with them. The commerce in Shanghai depends on the interior for sales. If the people in the interior cannot recover, they will have no purchasing power, and Shanghai will also be affected. We hope to raise one million this time for relief and distribution. Please donate generously.

Organizing an Inspection Group

After the representatives of the three provinces reported,

the discussion turned to the progress of fundraising and inspection of disaster areas, but because many committee members were not present, a decision on fundraising methods could not be made. As for the organization of the inspection group, the entire meeting agreed to nominate Wang Yansong, Wang Laixiao, Wen Lanting, Zhao Jinqing, Liu Zhanen, Huang Hanzhi, Ye Yuhu, Yu Xiji, and Pan Gongzhan as members of the preparatory committee. The committee will be located at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. In the future, any organizations or journalists in Shanghai who wish to understand the truth of the situation there can contact the preparatory committee and join them.

Chiang's Telegram Requesting Inspection

General Commander Chiang requested the various circles in Shanghai to organize an inspection group to inspect the recovered areas of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei: The Shanghai Temporary Relief Association for the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Disaster Areas (omission) has received the telegram with respect. The communist bandit areas recovered in Henan, Anhui, and Hubei have been in a state of decline for a long time, and the disaster situation is severe. I am deeply grateful for your compassion and concern for the remaining people, and for your organization of a temporary relief association to prepare for the urgent relief of farmers and workers in the disaster areas. I admire your benevolent reputation. I hope that you will organize a group as soon as possible to inspect the disaster areas, design a detailed plan, and start implementation. I also urge you to actively raise relief funds. Once a certain amount has been collected, please inform the headquarters by telegram so that we can consider the disaster situation and allocate the funds. This is a special reply. I respectfully hope that you will take note of it. Chiang Kai-shek, seal.

Chiang's Telegram Appealing for Relief

General Commander Chiang telegraphed, appealing for relief for the areas affected by the bandits in Henan, Anhui, and Hubei: The Relief Committee of the National Government, charitable organizations, leaders, universities, and newspapers are all informed. I, Chiang Kai-shek, am ordered to be stationed in Hankou to suppress the Red bandits. Fortunately, the military and government, both high and low, are of one mind and work together to overcome obstacles and gradually eliminate the bandits. However, in the recovered areas, everything has been plundered. There is no house that has not been burned, no tree that has not been felled, no chickens or dogs left, and no cattle spared. According to reports from front-line generals in the past half-month, places such as Shangcheng, Guangshan, and Gushi in Henan, Liu'an, Huoqiu, Huoshan, and Yingshan in Anhui, and Huang'an, Macheng, Luotian, Mianyang, and Jianli in Hubei are all remote areas, desolate and devoid of smoke. Only the sound of weeping can be heard. Thousands or even tens of thousands of people are kneeling before the army, emaciated and haggard, lying on the side of the road. After reading these reports, I was heartbroken. I have already telegraphed the governments of the three provinces to expedite the relief and send personnel to provide assistance. I have also promulgated measures to reduce or exempt land taxes in the bandit suppression areas for compliance, in order to provide stability. However, the recovered areas have been in a state of decline for a long time, and the disaster is deep. There are many people waiting for relief, and the areas in need of relief are extensive. The relief funds are limited, and the relief is minimal. Winter is coming soon, and it is unbearable to imagine death from freezing and starvation. I deeply believe that when hunger and cold reach the body, even a loving mother cannot protect her child. Since ancient times, famine has been the source of great chaos, and after great chaos is pacified, it is followed by famine. These are mutually causal. If we do not properly plan for the aftermath, local stability and the restoration of order will never be possible. Therefore, I hope that people's organizations, charitable institutions, and wealthy households will do their best to collect large sums of money for relief, and report the amount collected to the headquarters for verification and allocation. You should know that in this time of disasters, to save oneself, one must first save others. If the country is not peaceful, how can the family be protected? You should also know that saving people is not just a matter of compassion, but also a matter of duty. You should actively donate to give the survivors hope of rebirth, to share joys and sorrows equally, and to give society a chance to recover. The misfortunes, blessings, safety, and danger are shared by the people of the whole country. Furthermore, since the outbreak of the war, not only has the turmoil been more severe than in the past, but also frugality has been less than in the past. The cities are becoming more and more extravagant, and the suffering of the countryside is deepening. If this trend continues, even without foreign troubles, we will not be able to avoid ruin. I also hope that leaders of all schools and organizations, as well as women's circles, will organize inspection groups to visit the disaster areas in batches to understand the truth and seek relief. The headquarters will pay attention to protection and provide convenience during their inspection trips. The whole country should be aware of this tragedy and promote simplicity and frugality, eliminate extravagance, restore the countryside, and promote the sale of agricultural products, which is the common goal and path for our people to follow. I hope you will give it careful consideration. Chiang Kai-shek, 30th secret.

Feng Yuxiang Telegraphed Luo to Refute Rumors

Hua Dong News Agency reports that since Feng Yuxiang left Mount Tai and went to Zhangjiakou, rumors have spread like wildfire. I have received your telegram with respect. Since I have been recuperating, I have had very little news other than reading. Moreover, my history and thoughts are well known to you. In the past, I denounced the restoration of the monarchy, drove away Puyi, overthrew the warlords, and opposed dictatorship. How could I today make the mistake of supporting Duan Qirui and restoring the monarchy? As for the second item, regarding the infighting between Lu Zhonglin and others, and the banditry of the communists, I am not in power and cannot answer on their behalf. This matter is extremely relevant to the National Government's international standing. I hope you can refute it. This is a special reply. Your brother, Feng Yuxiang, respectfully.

The Sales Volume of the Shen Bao Monthly Magazine Has Increased Sharply

Ong Zhaoyuan's Memoirs of the Songhu Blood Battle Will Be Published as a Separate Volume

The Shen Bao Monthly Magazine, launched by the Shen Bao in July this year to commemorate its 60th anniversary, has been extremely well received by all sectors since its publication. Not long after publication, the first and second issues were sold out. After the reprint of the book in the middle of this month, it will also be sold out in less than two weeks. Because of the busy workload, the monthly magazine originally did not intend to print a third edition. However, the sales volume has recently increased sharply, and eight or nine out of ten subscribers have requested to subscribe from the first issue. Therefore, the magazine had no choice but to prepare to reprint the third edition of the first and second issues, and add prints of the second edition of the third and fourth issues to meet the needs of this year's commemorative subscribers. The fifth issue is still in printing, and the number of copies has been increased to avoid the trouble of reprinting in the future. In addition, Ong Zhaoyuan's Memoirs of the Songhu Blood Battle, which has been serialized in the magazine since the third issue, will be completed in the sixth issue. The separate volume will be published in early January next year as the first title in the Shen Bao Monthly Magazine series, and there will be a special price offer, which will be announced soon.
