Supplement to the Local Edition of Shen Bao

Speech

Knowing What's What

— Buddha

The night is late and people are quiet. Suddenly, in a deep alley, a narrow road, you hear the words, "Know what's what." There is not one person who isn't dumbfounded, their hair standing on end. Those who know what's what will take out the Yuan heads (money) and other items they have on them and offer them up with both hands. If you don't know what's what, you'll be made to regret it.

The words "knowing what's what" mean "to act according to circumstances" or "to read the wind." Observing the popularity of this term, one can understand the greatness of its effect. My friend Zhao Tagong has said, "When walking, pay attention to traffic lights; when living, learn from so-and-so." This is the meaning of knowing what's what. If something can be done, do it. If something cannot be done, don't do it—this is knowing what's what. If someone can be befriended, befriend them. If someone cannot be befriended, don't befriend them—this is knowing what's what. If someone can be talked to, talk to them. If someone cannot be talked to, don't talk to them—this too is knowing what's what.

When Group A gains power, I immediately turn around and align myself with Group A—this is knowing what's what. When Person B gains power, I immediately change my face and befriend Person B—this too is knowing what's what. The two words "knowing" seem easy, but are actually very difficult. If you do it improperly, knowing what's what will turn into not knowing what's what. The 19th Route Army's 5th Army resisting the violent Japanese seems like not knowing what's what, but because it's what the people desire, it is knowing what's what. The northern generals completely not resisting seems like knowing what's what, but because they are abandoned by the people, it is not knowing what's what.

I will further illustrate with two historical examples.

During the Warring States period, after Lord Mengchang was deposed, all his guests left. Later, he summoned them again. Lord Mengchang sighed and said, "I always treated my guests well, and never dared to neglect them. Now, seeing me deposed, they all turned their backs on me. If they were to see me again, they would surely spit in my face." This is an example of guests knowing and not knowing what's what.

Also, Wang Bo was orphaned and poor when he was young. He once stayed at the Magnolia Temple in Yangzhou and ate with the monks. The monks grew tired of him, so they would ring the bell after the meal was finished. Wang Bo would arrive only after they had already eaten. Twenty years later, Wang Bo was stationed in the same area. When he went to inscribe characters, he saw that the inscription was covered with a green gauze curtain. Wang Bo wrote a poem: "The sermon is over, and everyone has gone their separate ways. I am ashamed of the monk's bell after the meal. For twenty years, dust has covered my face. Only now do I have this green gauze covering." This too is an example of the monks knowing and not knowing what's what.

Hence the ancient saying, "Kissing the horse's rear instead of its head." Lord Mengchang's guests may have thought they knew what's what, but in the end, they did not. The monks were the most knowledgeable, but sometimes they too made mistakes. It's evident that knowing what's what is no easy matter. If one can know what's what in all places and in all matters, then one is truly talented.

Literature and Art

Gazing South at the Elms and Descendants

—

Dance academies rise in droves on the sea coast, all imitating foreign customs. A friend invited me to watch a dance, but I declined due to illness. To describe its nature, I compose this song. Alas, the entire nation is frenzied. With such a celestial demon singing across the river, why must a merchant's daughter's lament come from within? How can it be stopped?

Celestial demon dance, tapping rhythmically as if in response, drunk butterflies flying together in embraces, a startling goose step, each glance captivating, dissolving all sorrows of past and present,

Celestial demon dance, heaven and earth rise and fall, golden lotuses barely touching the ground, seeming about to rise, jade trees unable to stand straight in the wind, foreign melodies lingering,

Celestial demon dance, neither mist nor haze, burning phoenix strings urging the body to chase swallows, rhinoceros horn combs transforming into a pile of crows, waist drums beating ceaselessly,

Celestial demon dance, shadow vying with lightning, drunken eyes transforming the city in a daze, light body, naked country, walking in a dream, directly startling the butterfly's soul, (Records of the Grand Historian, Yu travels in a naked country)

Celestial demon dance, beauty and skill perfectly combined, foreign shirts tailored as thin as cicada wings, military attire leather-made, phoenix hooks sharp, paired 　 double plovers,

Celestial demon dance, cin

Several Types of Cosmetics

— Shen Erming

The following are several types of cosmetics, excerpted from the *Universal Library*. Considering the large readership of this publication, they are introduced below for general knowledge.

Face Powder

The main raw material for face powder used to be lead carbonate. However, lead carbonate is poisonous, and prolonged use will inevitably make the complexion ashen and bloodless. Therefore, zinc white (i.e., zinc oxide) is now mostly used instead. The following two types are both top-grade white powders:

㈠ Five hundred cubic centimeters of zinc oxide, three kilograms of precipitated calcium carbonate, five hundred cubic centimeters of talcum powder, one kilogram of starch, thirty cubic centimeters of jasmine essence, thirty cubic centimeters of rose essence, thirty cubic centimeters of orange blossom essence, and 7.5 cubic centimeters of musk essence. Grind the above four types of powder until extremely fine, sieve through a very fine sieve, and then mix. Slowly drip in the essences, adding and stirring simultaneously, not too quickly.

㈡ Seven hundred cubic centimeters of wheat starch, five hundred cubic centimeters of zinc oxide, four hundred cubic centimeters of talcum essence, ten cubic centimeters of sweet-osmanthus essence, and five cubic centimeters of rose essence. First, grind the powder finely, sieve, and mix, then add the fragrances.

Rouge

Rose Rouge Solution: Thirty-five cubic centimeters of fuchsine, sixty cubic centimeters of ammonium chloride solution, seventy cubic centimeters of rose essence, and two liters of rose water. First, grind the fuchsine into small pieces, put it in a bottle, add ammonium chloride solution, and shake repeatedly. After leaving it for several days, add rose essence and rose water, and shake even more. After eight days, take the clear liquid from the top, and you're done.

Rouge Paste: Thirty cubic centimeters of fuchsine, fifty cubic centimeters of powdered gum arabic, six hundred cubic centimeters of talcum powder, or an appropriate amount of rose oil. Place the above ingredients in a bowl, mix, and grind them. Add a small amount of water and mix into a thick paste.

Emulsion

Ordinary emulsion is a white liquid that does not contain free alkali. When used to wipe the face, it can make the skin clean, white, soft, and smooth, which is superior to pancreatic soap.

Glycerin Emulsion: Two hundred and fifty cubic centimeters of glycerin, four hundred cubic centimeters of almond oil, one hundred cubic centimeters of spermaceti, thirty-two cubic centimeters of beeswax (double the amount in summer), three hundred and fifty cubic centimeters of rose water, and four cubic centimeters of rose oil. Melt the beeswax and spermaceti in a porcelain dish, slowly add almond oil and rose water containing glycerin, and then add rose oil.

Freckle Emulsion: Fifty cubic centimeters of camphor, twenty cubic centimeters of ammonium oxide, ten cubic centimeters of mercuric chloride, one hundred cubic centimeters of egg white, and one kilogram of rose water. First, dissolve the camphor in a small amount of alcohol, then dissolve the ammonium oxide, mercuric chloride, and egg white separately in water. Slowly mix and stir, resulting in a white precipitate or emulsion. This is quite effective in treating freckles, but it is poisonous and should not be ingested.

Depilatory

Depilatories are medicines used to remove beards, chest hair, etc. They are generally sulfides of calcium, barium, etc. The effectiveness of old depilatories decreases, so newly prepared ones must be used. Depilatories can damage the skin, so caution should be exercised when using them.

㈠ Three cubic centimeters of barium sulfide, one cubic centimeter of starch, and an appropriate amount of water. Mix into a paste, apply to the skin, and wash off with water after the hair falls out.

㈡ Twelve cubic centimeters of alcohol, thirty-five cubic centimeters of collodion, 0.7 cubic centimeters of iodine, 1.5 cubic centimeters of turpentine, and two cubic centimeters of castor oil. Mix and apply thickly to the skin. ㈢ Eight cubic centimeters of quicklime powder, one cubic centimeter of carbonic acid , and one cubic centimeter of potassium sulfide. Mix with an appropriate amount of water and apply.

Hair Dye

Lead Acetate Hair Dye Solution: Three cubic centimeters of lead acetate, twelve cubic centimeters of sodium thiosulfate, thirty cubic centimeters of glycerin, thirty cubic centimeters of pure alcohol, and four hundred cubic centimeters of distilled water. First, dissolve the lead acetate and sodium thiosulfate separately in a small amount of water. Then, add the sodium thiosulfate solution to the mixture of alcohol, glycerin, and water, stirring constantly. Next, pour in the lead acetate solution. Store in a blue bottle. After one day, take the clear liquid and brush it on the hair once a day to gradually turn it black. However, it should not be used frequently, as lead is poisonous.

Gold Hair Solution: This is a nitrogen dioxide solution, which has bleaching power and can bleach hair into a golden yellow color. When using it for the first time, use a diluted solution and first wash the hair with pancreatic soap water. Then, wash off the pancreatic soap with clean water before applying it.

Potassium Permanganate Solution: One hundred and fifty cubic centimeters of potassium permanganate and two liters of distilled water. This is a brown hair dye and can also be used to dye the beard.

Hand Products

Hand cosmetics are used to apply to the hands to make the skin white and to polish the nails to make them smooth.

Hand Cream: Thirty cubic centimeters of hydrous lanolin, twenty cubic centimeters of glycerin, ten cubic centimeters of borax, two cubic centimeters of Yu Shu Shen Oil, and one cubic centimeter of bitter almond oil. Mix the above ingredients thoroughly and apply to the hands.

Nail Polishing Powder: One hundred cubic centimeters of zinc oxide, one hundred cubic centimeters of talcum powder, fifty cubic centimeters of starch, one cubic centimeter of fuchsine, two kilograms of finely powdered stannic oxide, ten cubic centimeters of bergamot oil, ten cubic centimeters of lavender oil, and twenty cubic centimeters of fuchsine. Mix.

Nail Polish: Two cubic centimeters of paraffin wax and sixty cubic centimeters of petroleum ether. Dissolve the paraffin wax in petroleum ether, then dye it peach-red with alkanet root. When using, dip a brush in it and apply it to the nails.

Parents, Stop Arguing

Society Improvement Discussion Group

Conclusions on Improving Family Problems

— Cimin

Although Messrs. Yun Zong, Ming Xing, Zhuo Yun, and Wen Bing have successively expressed their opinions in this publication regarding the issue of improving the family, their arguments have only considered one aspect of the problem, failing to take the whole into account. As a result, the issue has been delayed until now without a proper solution, which is truly regrettable.

Within their respective arguments, all premised on a shared agreement regarding the inadequacy of the family system, we can clearly discern two divergent tendencies:

1. The family is a constituent element of society, and the corruption of society is rooted in the inadequacy of the family system. Therefore, improving the family is the initial step in improving society. This "small to large" argument is advocated by Messrs. Yun Zong and Zhuo Yun.

2. The family cannot exist independently of the social system. The inadequacy of the family system stems from the inadequacy of the social, economic, and political systems. Therefore, improving the family requires first improving the organization of society's politics and economy. This "large to small" argument is advocated by Messrs. Ming Xing and Wen Bing.

The first viewpoint only grasps the point that an inadequate family system can exert a negative influence on society, completely ignoring the social foundation that produces this family system. The second viewpoint, on the other hand, does the reverse, only explaining the social organization from which an inadequate family system arises, completely erasing the point that the inadequate family system exerts a negative influence on society.

That is why I say that they have only seen one aspect of the problem, failing to take the whole into account. I believe that the establishment of a family system is entirely dependent on the social organization. For example, a feudal social organization produces a large family system of clustered clans, and a capitalist social organization produces a small family system of monogamous couples. The current "neither fish nor fowl" social organization in our country has given rise to a mix of small families and large families. . . [illegible text] . . . It is definitely not what Yun Zong and Zhuo Yun advocate. However, although the production of the family system depends on the lower-level social organization, once the family system is established, it inevitably can and does exert many influences on the social, political, and economic systems from which it originates. There are already many such examples. It is also inappropriate that Messrs. Wen Bing dismiss this lightly.

Here, I list the mutual relationship between the two as follows:

Upper Level: Family System | Lower Level: Social Organization

Therefore, if we want to thoroughly improve the family, we must wait for the improvement of the social organization. In the process of improving the social organization, we cannot get rid of the influence given by the family.

This is my humble opinion. I hope the editor and readers will further instruct me!

Short Story

The Harm of Gambling

— Yixin

A Scene of Sorrow in a Telephone

Characters:

The Eldest Brother (Suicide Attempt - Not on Stage), The Second Brother, The Third Brother, The Third Brother's Wife

Object: Telephone

Location: This City

Time: 4:00 AM

Scene opens with the Third Brother and his wife sound asleep in bed. The Second Brother calls.

(Telephone) Ring... ring... ring...

(The Third Brother's Wife) The ringing sound reaches her ears, and she wakes up, saying: "Who would be calling at this hour?" (Calling her husband) "Hey, the phone's ringing! Get up and answer it quickly!"

(The Third Brother) Woken up by his wife, also hears the ringing of the telephone. He gets up in a fluster, saying resentfully: "Who's calling at this ungodly hour?" He shuffles out in his slippers to answer it. "Hello, hello, who is this?"

(The Second Brother) "Hello, is this the Third Brother? It's me, the Second Brother."

(The Third Brother) "Yes, it's me. Is that you, Second Brother? Hello, hello, what's the matter that you're calling at this hour?"

(The Second Brother) "Hello, hello, I'm calling to tell you that the Eldest Brother died last night. Please come over quickly."

(The Third Brother) "The Eldest Brother is dead? Hello, hello, what disease did he have? How could he die so quickly?"

(The Second Brother) "Hello, he didn't have any disease. He committed suicide by taking poison."

(The Third Brother) "Ah! What kind of stimulation did he suffer that he committed suicide?"

(The Second Brother) "Hello, around a little past one o'clock last night, I was sound asleep when someone from his house came to call me. I asked him why he was calling me? He said: 'The Eldest Brother has taken poison.' He was already suffering from the poison and told me to quickly come and find a way. When I heard that, I braved the chilling wind and immediately ran to his house. He was in bed shouting in pain, 'It hurts so much! It hurts so much!' I asked him, 'Big Brother, why did you do this?' I asked him several times. He opened his eyes and looked at me a few times, tears streaming down his face, and said to me: 'Ah! Second Brother, I can't go on living.' After saying that, he stopped talking. I asked him repeatedly again. He said: 'I lost several thousand dollars in the XX gambling company. This several thousand dollars was still from the shop's promissory notes. I privately issued a promissory note ... [illegible text] ...I was momentarily confused, now it's too late... After thinking it over and over, suicide is easier. After I die, please arrange for you and the Third Brother to take care of those children and look after them.' As he spoke, his voice grew softer and softer, and it was hard to hear clearly. At that moment, I forgot about the question of saving him, and quickly called a rickshaw and sent him to the hospital. After the doctor gave him a stomach pumping, I asked the doctor if there was any hope of saving him from the poison. The doctor said that he had taken too much poison and that it would be difficult to save him. Sure enough, before three hours had passed, he shouted 'Ah!' and died. Hello, hello, come over quickly!"

(Telephone) Cuts off.

(The Third Brother) "Ah! Ah! Big Brother, I repeatedly told you not to gamble, but you gambled more and more. Now you've abandoned us like this, how can I not be heartbroken?"

(The Third Brother's Wife) "Hey, who was calling on the phone for so long?" (The Third Brother) "The Second Brother called to tell me that the Eldest Brother died."

(The Third Brother's Wife) "Ah, I ran into him on the street a couple of days ago, and he even greeted me with a smile. Why would he die for no reason? What disease did he die from?"

(The Third Brother) "Ah, he committed suicide because he lost several thousand dollars gambling. Isn't it pitiful that he died so tragically?"

(The Third Brother's Wife) "Gambling is the most terrible thing. Losing money goes without saying, but he even lost his life. I've always told you, no matter what kind of gambling, you can't gamble. Small gambling wastes time, large gambling leads to ruin. Now it's clear. He's telling you to go quickly, why are you still standing there dumbly?"

(The Third Brother) Hearing his wife's words, he hurriedly put on his clothes and went out.

Valuing Clothes Over People

A Silk Pongee Robe

— Wu

Recently, I made myself a silk pongee robe. Because in this society where "clothes are valued over people," I believe that a valuable garment can be of great help to me.

Because of my poor clothing, I have been ridiculed by many people. Once, when I went to the XX Hall on business, I boldly entered the elevator and said to the operator:

"Third floor."

But the operator looked me up and down and said angrily:

"What? You want to take the elevator to the third floor? Go to the fifth floor!"

Under this shout, I went all the way up to the fifth floor. Without saying a word, I had to walk down step by step from the fifth floor. Alas! After all, I don't have a generous mind. I sighed deeply.

From then on, I worked hard to save a few dollars and actually bought a piece of silk pongee material worth twelve dollars. Coming back from the main street, I felt extremely happy. I thought: "Now I can get rich." At dinner, my wife asked me:

"Then what material will we use for the lining?"

"Ah! That's right, it still needs a lining." I suddenly realized.

But where would the money come from? This really made things difficult for me. So I had to borrow from others, but no one had any money on hand. [illegible text] Finally, I was fortunate enough to borrow one yuan from a friend and bought the lining and also prepared the tailor's wages.

Yesterday, I wore this new lined robe and walked onto XX Street. I took the elevator to the third floor and then walked down halfway. The driver just smiled without saying a word. I guessed that he must be thinking:

"Ah! This is a new silk pongee robe."

So I felt victorious.

But today, unfortunately, an ignorant child unexpectedly peed on me. This is such a big loss for me! So I saw the child's bottom being beaten red by my wife, and large tears fell from her long eyelashes.

Of course, I had to carefully take it to the laundry to be washed. It cost me two dimes to wash and iron it clean, but the faded traces remained conspicuously. Alas! A silk pongee lined robe worth more than ten dollars! ... Maybe this is my fate!

Family Problems

Brave Women's Army

— Huoren

This morning at six o'clock, I picked up a country gentleman from the Ning Shao Wharf. Because I didn't have any luggage, I didn't hire a car. Talking and chatting, I walked along the sandy road. When I walked to a street on Zhonghua Road, I saw many people looking into a house. I didn't know what they were looking at. I also walked closer. I only heard the sound of breaking bowls and plates. After a while, it changed to the sound of slapping tables and knocking chairs. Looking into the crowd, they were already fighting fiercely. It was a woman who was beating and scolding, "You rotten slut! You demon! I was charmed by you for two or three nights, you've been hiding your dirty deeds from me. This morning, your lewd tricks were revealed!"

After scolding for a while, she angrily grabbed a man in his forties by the chest and dragged him out, saying, "Come with me to home!" She scolded as she escorted the man away. Seeing the man enduring it with his head down, he must be very afraid of his wife.

Inside the house, there was a woman of about twenty years old. This woman was indeed very beautiful. [illegible text] yesterday's romantic affair: disheveled hair, [illegible text], still fresh, also scolded with a crisp voice: ... [illegible text] ...

From the bystanders, I learned that this woman was the man's concubine.

His wife, because the man had not been home for several nights, tried hard to find out. She rented a house in this place and kept a concubine. Hearing this news, the wife was overcome with jealousy. She came early in the morning to seize the bedding and was indeed able to catch them. After they left, my friend and I also left.

Alas! ... Now, internally and externally, the country is in a crisis, a time to "sleep on brushwood and taste gall." It is pitiful ... that the wealthy compatriots are still indulging in pleasure in the arms of their concubines. Alas! Alas! How can there be a country for them? Where is there a time for "sleeping on brushwood and tasting gall"?

I hope that the wives of men who take concubines will work hard to train a women's army and strive to be a "He Dong Lion's Roar"!

Overseas News

Changes in Film and Drama Style

— Rongke

Recently, a change has occurred in the film and drama industry. Social love and gangster fight films that were once popular will soon become relics of the past. The scripts of the former divine and majestic silent films such as *The Ten Commandments*, *The King of Kings*, *The Battle of Flowers*, and *Ben-Hur* will rise again in response to the times.

Social love and gangster fights are common in everyday life. Repeating them in movies will inevitably make the general audience tired of them over time. Audiences psychologically prefer romantic and heroic historical dramas with sound and color from ancient times. Winning the heart of a beautiful woman with a long sword is much more interesting than sweeping with a machine gun. At least, this is the idea of ​​the great director Cecil B. DeMille.

With this idea, DeMille directed a great new film called *The Sign of the Cross*. His eyes are full of enthusiasm for creating this epic film. He told people, "I believe people are tired of watching the popular films and will be disgusted. I will forget the sounds and colors that we see and hear now and describe the glorious history of Rome thousands of years ago. When you watch *The Sign of the Cross*, you will not only get a glimpse of Rome, but you will feel like you are seeing Rome during the reign of Emperor Nero with your own eyes. In this new film, everything in Rome during the Nero era will be completely and truly unfolded before your eyes, scene by scene. Among them is the most beautiful love story that has never been described before. Because the most brilliant gem becomes a dead thing without a proper background, I describe the love story of Marcus and Mercia against the most magnificent background ever created in a film."

DeMille was talking in a room scattered with countless sets used in the film. The huge books piled up prove his research work in creating this new film. People who hear DeMille speak and point cannot help but be moved by his passionate personality and strong ideas. In his eloquent account, people seem to see the great sights of the Roman city again. When Nero is in the palace, and in the arena, on the blood-stained soil, people see the bodies of Christian martyrs being torn apart by the claws of hungry lions to provide entertainment for the Romans.

The glory, strength, brutality, and treachery of Rome are all seen with the naked eye. These characteristics will be captured in *The Sign of the Cross* in the future and become a terrible and beautiful epic script.

Miss Li Youci, Female Normal School Graduate, Excels in Swimming and Dancing

Film Review

The Charming One

— Suyi

*Le Chaland* by Parisian students is currently being screened at the Lanxin Grand Theater. *Le Chaland* directly translates to (The Charming One). It is a sound film evolved from a French musical. In terms of plot, the life of Parisian university students described in the play is not fully reflected. The unique scenery of the Latin Quarter (Quartier Latin), the various oddities of Boulevard Saint-Michel (Boulevard St Miche), and the romantic life of university students have not been depicted. Cheating on written and oral exams in major exams is also not entirely reasonable.

In terms of insertion, there are light songs and wonderful dances. The male protagonist, Henry Garat, was originally from a musical theater and has something in common with the world-renowned Chevalier. The female protagonist, Lemmouniere, was originally an actress in a Parisian musical theater (Folie Bere), so the pairing is not too far-fetched. All other roles are dancers from the famous Parisian musical theater (Folie Bere). Scene after scene is inserted, like a series of short-act musicals popular in Paris. So, in simple words, this play is a sound film changed from an opera.

There are several commendable designs in this play: One point is the angels that jump out of the ink bottles on the desks and the many fairies that roll out of the Roman law books that the dissipated university students see in their dreams the night before the exam, circling around on the desk; one point is that a couple is talking under the statues of many celebrities in the university courtyard, and the heads of the statues will dance and sing; and one point is that the people in the paintings on the wall will also wave fans and sing. These don't have any great principles, but the beauty lies in thinking about the unthinkable.

Introduction to Domestic Films

The Rise of Hunting Films

— Yannan

Film is an art produced by the times, so it must follow the times. The old detective films, romance films, ethical films, war and love films, martial arts films, etc., have all fallen behind. Even the song and dance films of one or two years ago have declined. From 1932, what is needed is stimulation, terror, and tension. As a result, hunting films have received a superior position.

This trend has only been popular for a year. Let's take a look, from *Human Beasts* to *Ape Tiger*, *African Little People*, *Tarzan the Ape Man*, *Strange Beasts*, and *Ice Country Spectacle*, which one does not have the great power to be called a hit? Therefore, it is predicted that there will definitely be more of these films produced in large quantities in the future.

The first to advocate shooting Chinese hunting films was Huang Qizha. He was originally an innovator in running film magazines and is now working at Yilian Company. He plans to make six of these epic films. This publication has repeatedly introduced them before, so let's take a look at other companies.

The Times Film Company is a new organization, and perhaps many people don't know about it? Strangely enough, the production of the first film took the path of the times. Called *Going to the Wilderness*, it is directed by Zhu Xuehua and stars the famous dancing star Ms. Li Li. It is said that it will be published soon, and may be ahead of Yilian Company.

There is also *The Story of the Wild Man on the Desert Island*, which was filmed earlier than the Times Company. It is produced by the Happy Forest Company and stars Xu Suzhen and Tang Xueqian. We certainly know that Ms. Xu and Tang are famous figures in Chinese martial arts films. However, the Happy Forest Company is quite unfamiliar. Moreover, there is also a good dog in this film, called Qie Li, just like Rin Tin Tin and Ming Ge. This is also a domestic film innovation.

Good news is coming! Her first sound film *Paradise Bird* has arrived in Shanghai! Her English carries her native accent, which we won't find annoying. Because Chevalier, doesn't he have a French accent? But we find it more lovely than pure English. This film is produced by RKO and is a masterpiece by the famous director King Vidor. The male protagonist is Zoey McRea. The film has arrived in Shanghai, and many people must be looking forward to it. But this is unfortunate. The old theater owners know that this is a hot commodity, and everyone is working hard to compete for rental, so it has not been officially resolved until now. I don't know which lucky theater will win!

However, it won't be delayed for many more days. We will soon be able to see this Spanish girl on the screen! And she also spoke!

Foreign Essays

A Discussion on the Trend of Soviet Films in the Last Fifteen Years (Continued)

— Shi Yi

｜Based on the Opinions of Harry Alan Potamkin｜

The Soviet film, judging by the increasing strength of its progress, can be inferred to become a new realistic and brilliant aspect of Soviet culture. Such an observation may seem like an exaggerated assumption, but I can justify it with a borrowed idiom, (ideological rearmament).

What role should Soviet films occupy? The answer to this question aligns with the evolution of Soviet society. In the initial fourteen years of the Soviet Union, the various necessary and pressing social relationships have now been dissolved into new opportunities and destroyed by the successful establishment of the social system. The steel framework of social structure has already been erected. What is currently needed is to build human diversity upon it. The importance of film in this endeavor is as significant as its importance in the foundation of society because this significance involves rearming the Soviet people with a more precise intellectual arsenal. We can also say that this is the general direction of filmmaking.

Douglas's Skills

— Bu Min

Douglas Fairbanks's skills are indeed impressive. Some people say, look, when Los Angeles, USA, held the World Olympic Games, other self-proclaimed stars came to the Olympic Village, strutting around and looking around, but foreign athletes ignored them, and they left feeling bored. But when Fairbanks came, the situation was different. Everyone shouted, "Isn't that Douglas?" So everyone gathered around, took out their diaries, and asked him to sign them as a souvenir. What an honor this is! Because these athletes from all over the world have seen Fairbanks's swordsmanship, boxing, and flying leaps in films. How could they not recognize him upon meeting him today? But a few days ago, when Fairbanks arrived in Shanghai, he told people a story. He said that one day, the American golf champion Jones was playing golf in Hollywood, with countless spectators. Fairbanks himself also went to play golf. Soon, the countless spectators were watching Jones and Fairbanks. Jones felt quite embarrassed. Douglas tells this story to everyone, taking great pride in it. However, Douglas has played golf in Shanghai for several days, losing every match. It is evident that although Douglas creates a sensation everywhere, he truly has the ability to create sensations, and doesn't necessarily need to be superior in martial arts or sports.

Reader's Opinions

Review of "Adorable Enemies"

— Li Ling

"Adorable Enemies" is such a moving theme. I was drawn by this title and excitedly went to the Central Theater. I wanted to know the story and also admire Mr. Cheng Bugao's new work. I never bother watching domestic films. It's not that I despise domestic films, but I feel it's a waste of money, time, and energy, and you really can't get anything out of it. In other words, I don't need to watch domestic films. However, this time, I unexpectedly gained considerable satisfaction. I left the theater happily, ran home happily, and felt a kind of feeling happily. I felt that China's film industry is progressing day by day. How gratifying and comforting this is!

I will now write down what I have seen and thought.

The script of "Adorable Enemies" does not have much meaning. Perhaps the author's intention was only to expose the pursuit of love by modern young men and women, while also telling us how sincere friendship can be.

The structure of the play is an ordinary and lengthy story, and it is clearly a microcosm of modern student life. It does not seem to have enough power for society or the youth of today. However, the subject matter of the play is very novel. Although it lacks artistic value, it can be considered a rare gem compared to the current Chinese film scripts.

I had seen one of Cheng Bugao's works before, (Falling Rosy Clouds and a Lonely Wild Duck), but I didn't get any good impression. (Adorable Enemies) can be said to be Mr. Cheng Bugao's unprecedented masterpiece. What I admire most in the whole film is that it is not dull anywhere, and there are many places where the acting talent can be revealed, such as the scene where Zhao Youcheng and Xu Yuanlu snatch the photograph, and the shooting angle when Xu Yuanlu silently thinks on Zhao Youcheng's empty bed after graduation. One can see the director's skills. However, this film is not perfect. There are several places that are unreasonable. Now I will give two of the most obvious examples.

1. After Xu Yuanlu stole the watch, how could he even forget to untie the rope that he had hung up himself? How could anyone be so careless?

2. Zhao Youcheng was hit by the watchman and fell from the wall, desperately fleeing without getting entangled with the watchman. Why was there clearly another scene during the re-release? There are many other minor flaws, but in the current Chinese film industry, where everything is subject to material constraints, we should forgive them.

Next, I want to talk about the actors. The best actor is Gong Jianong, who acts very meticulously without the slightest forcedness. Although Zheng Xiaoqiu's Xu Yuanlu is lively and lovely, some places still feel insufficient, and the expressions are too poor.

Liang Saizhen and Wang Zhengxin don't look like students, or perhaps the two are not suitable for playing this kind of role.

The rest of the actors are neither good nor particularly bad. In summary, this play can be considered one of the better domestic films. Written in Jinglu on November 2nd.

Legs Became Feet

— Xing

"Million Dollar Legs", when released in Japan, was called "Million Dollar Feet" because the Japanese film censors are a group of very upright and unyielding people, and anything related to limbs is generally prohibited, especially legs worth a million dollars.

Film Treatise

China's Own Standard of Beauty

— Chen Dabei

Beginners in calligraphy inevitably trace red characters. In the past, Chinese films were nothing more than buying American red character templates and tracing them. Now we must quickly abandon the red character templates and find the most suitable calligraphy models to imitate. Where are our calligraphy models? Ha! This fits perfectly with the old saying (Far away at the horizon, but close at hand). We don't need to buy our calligraphy models from the outside. To study the art of performance on the screen, everywhere that humans exist is a calligraphy model we can imitate. In your study, in your home, in the homes of your relatives and friends, on the tram, on the train, on the road, in the streets and alleys, where isn't there a calligraphy model you can admire? What is your goal? Isn't it to perform? The secret of performance lies in reflecting society and revealing life. All the major events revealed in society, and even all the subtle details, which one is not a good source of information worth us studying carefully and imitating diligently?

The performance art of Charlie Chaplin, Lillian Gish, and Jannings were all honed and refined from their own environments. They did not come from imitating each other like we did in the past. We must perform the art that we have honed and refined from our own environments on the screen, so that they know that we Chinese are not all shrinking, hunched, queue-wearing, hoof-sleeved oriental monsters. At the same time, we can also let our compatriots see that we don't need drooping eyebrows, sunken eyes, high noses, or curly hair. We have our own oriental, Chinese standard of beauty. This is the most important work in the creative period that we urgently need to realize now.
